# Engram macOS — Alignment Design (close the 144 flow-review gaps)

**Date:** 2026-06-14 · **Source review:** `docs/reviews/ux-flow-review-2026-06-14.md` · **Branch:** `ux-flow-alignment`

Produced by an 18-WP design workflow (56 agents) with per-WP adversarial critique + revision. Amended after human sign-off on scope decisions (see *Decisions* below).

## Human decisions (2026-06-14)

1. **Misleading/no-op controls → DELETE.** semantic/hybrid search-mode selector + embedding pill (WP04), dead embedding status on Home/popover (WP09), no-op Strict-single-writer + unread Bearer/CIDR fields + wrong `/mcp` URL (WP12).
2. **Observability → fix + gate, and BUILD real telemetry (WP20).** Do NOT delete Performance/Traces — fill them with real data. Fix log reader / warn filter / redaction, and gate the whole surface behind a default-off *Developer Tools* flag (WP17).
3. **Pull into THIS round:** per-dollar **cost dashboard (WP19)** and **real Observability telemetry (WP20)**. Budget/threshold controls become honest by WIRING them to real cost data (not deleting). `linkSessions` arbitrary-linking stays deferred (WP07 ships `setParentSession` limb only).

## Execution waves

18 work-packages align the Engram macOS app's UI surface with its actual Swift service backend, organized into 4 execution waves where same-wave WPs own strictly disjoint files. The binding constraint is the service-layer cluster {WP05, WP06, WP13, WP16}: all four edit EngramServiceReadProvider.swift and three (06/13/16) also edit EngramServiceModels.swift, so they must be fully serialized into four separate waves. Wave 1 lands the foundational wire-ups and honesty cleanups (session actions, search-to-transcript, Memory page + service models, Home/popover, Projects, Settings, Observability). Wave 2 builds on Wave 1 outputs (Favorites/load-more depends on WP01's SessionsPageView edits; Replay backfill, Agents, Hygiene handler, Restart/FDA onboarding, and palette/token additions all reuse files freed by Wave 1). Wave 3 runs dashboards drill-in, Sources read-only surface, and cost deep-link in parallel. Wave 4 is WP16 alone (Hooks/Skills), forced after WP13 because both contend for the same two service files and WP16's full closure also depends on WP06's MemoryView refresh. Most findings are wire-up (backend exists, add UI entry); a smaller set is remove-misleading (dead semantic/hybrid controls, no-op Network/Web-security settings, Performance/Traces tabs) and one true backfill (WP05 Replay role/timestamps). The remove-misleading deletions of user-visible controls and the explicit deferrals (real Observability telemetry, linkSessions limb, orphan dollar/budget controls) are the items the human must confirm before implementation, since they are scope judgments rather than mechanical wiring.

- **Wave 1:** WP01, WP03, WP04, WP06, WP09, WP11, WP12, WP17 — Foundational wave; all 8 are pairwise file-disjoint. WP06 is the first occupant of the service-layer cluster (it edits EngramServiceReadProvider + Models + CommandHandler), so the other cluster members (05/13/16) and the CommandHandler co-tenant (14) are held out. WP03 takes MainWindowView + CommandPaletteView-adjacent + AppNotifications, so WP18 (MainWindow/Palette) and WP15 (AppNotifications) are deferred to Wave 2. WP01 takes TimelinePageView, so WP10 (also Timeline) is deferred. WP04 takes CommandPaletteView+SearchPageView. WP09/WP11/WP12/WP17 touch only their own files. This wave unblocks WP02 (needs WP01's SessionsPageView load-more+skeleton) and WP16 (needs WP06's MemoryView refresh).
- **Wave 2:** WP02, WP05, WP07, WP14, WP15, WP18 — All 6 pairwise file-disjoint and every cross-file collision with Wave 1 is now resolved. WP02 (Screen + new FavoritesPageView) depends on WP01 having shipped the SessionsPageView load-more trigger and SkeletonRow convention. WP05 is the cluster's second occupant of EngramServiceReadProvider (now free after WP06). WP14 takes EngramServiceCommandHandler (free after WP06). WP15 takes AppNotifications (free after WP03). WP18 takes MainWindowView + CommandPaletteView (free after WP03/WP04). WP07 takes Engram/Core/Database.swift, holding WP10 (also Database) to Wave 3.
- **Wave 3:** WP10, WP13, WP08 — Pairwise disjoint. WP10 needs TimelinePageView (free after WP01) and Engram/Core/Database.swift (free after WP07). WP13 is the third occupant of EngramServiceReadProvider + EngramServiceModels (free after WP05/WP06). WP08 is independent (UsagePressureNotifier + PopoverUsageSection) and balances the wave. WP13 and WP16 both edit Models + ReadProvider, so they cannot share a wave — WP16 is pushed to Wave 4.
- **Wave 4:** WP16 — WP16 edits EngramServiceModels + EngramServiceReadProvider, which WP13 holds in Wave 3, so it must follow. Its full closure of xc-events-nav-4 (Hooks/Skills/Memory refresh) also depends on WP06's MemoryView refresh from Wave 1. Single WP, trivially disjoint.

> Token-ordering fix (design open-decision #9, resolved by lead): the two shared tokens `Theme.cornerRadius` + `SourceColors.longLabel` (WP18) are pulled into a **Wave-0 micro-step** so Wave-1 consumers (WP01/WP09/WP12) reference a token that already exists.

**Amendments from decisions:** WP04/WP09/WP12 delete (confirmed). WP17 no longer deletes Perf/Traces — it does log-fix + Developer-Tools gating only; the telemetry that fills Perf/Traces is **WP20 (new)**. **WP19 (new)** adds the cost dashboard and wires the budget/threshold controls WP08/WP12 had flagged. WP19+WP20 join the serialized service-file cluster (EngramServiceReadProvider/Models/CommandHandler/Protocol/Client) and are scheduled after WP06's DTO/IPC base lands.

## Risks (from design)

Highest-leverage risk is the service-layer serialization chain WP06 to WP05 to WP13 to WP16: it spans all 4 waves and is the longest critical path, so any slip in EngramServiceReadProvider/Models work delays the tail. Mitigate by landing WP06's Models/Protocol/Client additions cleanly first since 05/13/16 extend the same DTOs. Second risk: WP01 is a prerequisite for WP02 (SessionsPageView load-more + SkeletonRow) AND it co-owns TimelinePageView with WP10 — the orchestrator must NOT mark sessions-browse-2/-6 or xc-states-3 closed when WP02 lands, because the Sessions-list first-load fix is WP01's edit; this hand-off boundary is easy to mis-track. Third: WP18 and WP09/WP01/WP12 share visual tokens — WP18 only ADDS the cornerRadius/longLabel tokens to Theme/SourceColors; the call-site application is handed to WP09/WP01 (Wave 1, before the token exists) and WP12 (Wave 1), so those call sites must define or inline the token defensively or WP18's token must move earlier. This is a latent ordering bug worth flagging: token producer (WP18, Wave 2) is AFTER token consumers (WP09/WP01/WP12, Wave 1). Recommend either pulling the two-token Theme/SourceColors addition into Wave 1 as a micro-WP, or having consumers inline the literal and WP18 refactor to the token. Fourth: remove-misleading deletions in WP04/WP12/WP17 also repair guard tests (cutover scan, UITests) in the same package — if the test repair is skipped the suite goes red; each such WP must land its test edit atomically.

## Disposition breakdown

Pure wire-up (backend exists, add the UI entry / call existing client method): WP01, WP02, WP03, WP06, WP07, WP15, WP16, WP18 — these are the majority and the safest. Backfill-data: WP05 only (Replay role/timestamps/tool-calls must be captured by EngramServiceReadProvider so the density bar and playback timing are real); scoped and safe, implement now. Mixed (wire-up + remove-misleading + possible defer in one package): WP04, WP08, WP09, WP10, WP11, WP12, WP13, WP14, WP17. Remove-misleading deletions that touch USER-VISIBLE controls (the honest fix is to remove/gate, NOT build the backend) — these need human sign-off: WP04 deletes the dead semantic/hybrid search-mode selector and embedding pill (CLAUDE.md confirms sqlite-vec is NOT implemented; search is keyword-only); WP09 removes dead embedding status from Home/popover; WP12 removes no-op Network/Web-security settings controls and fixes the misleading MCP URL; WP17 removes the Performance and Traces tabs (no telemetry backend). DEFERRED (genuinely out-of-scope, documented not built): WP17 real Observability telemetry collection (only honesty cleanup + log-reader fix is in scope); WP08 orphan dollar/budget controls (honestly deferred/handed off, only the pressure-notification deep-link + USAGE empty state ship); WP07 linkSessions limb of xc-capability-matrix-6 (only the setParentSession limb ships); WP02 insight create/delete UI half of xc-capability-matrix-1 (separate Memory-page feature, partly covered by WP06); WP11 replaces non-shipping `engram` CLI guidance with honest in-app copy rather than building the CLI.

---

## Work-packages

### WP01 — Session actions: wire Resume/Handoff/Replay/Copy + Hide/Unhide/Rename/Export/Favorite into the card menu and browse pages

- **Disposition:** wire-up  ·  **Critique:** needs-revision (revised)
- **Closes:** sessions-browse-1, xc-deadends-1, replay-4, session-actions-1, session-actions-2, session-actions-3, xc-deadends-2, xc-deadends-3, xc-deadends-5, xc-capability-matrix-3, xc-capability-matrix-4, xc-capability-matrix-5, sessions-browse-3, sessions-browse-4, hygiene-5, xc-capability-matrix-9
- **Goal:** Make every session-card context-menu item and every shipped session write-API actually do something from the two primary browse surfaces (Sessions, Timeline). Resume/Copy-Resume-Command/Handoff/Replay stop being silent no-ops, and Hide/Unhide/Rename/Export/Favorite-toggle become reachable from the card menu, all by calling EngramServiceClient methods and sheet/notification paths that already exist and are already wired in SessionDetailView/HomeView. recordSessionAccess fires on resume/open. No backend is built.
- **Approach:** The root cause is a closure-passing gap, not a missing backend. ExpandableSessionCard already declares onResume/onCopyResumeCommand/onHandoff/onReplay/onConfirmSuggestion/onDismissSuggestion optional closures and renders the 4-item contextMenu on both the parent row (lines 116-129) and CompactChildRow (lines 342-355), but SessionsPageView (lines 67-80) and TimelinePageView (lines 84-96) construct the card passing only onTap/onChildTap/onConfirmSuggestion/onDismissSuggestion — so the headline actions optional-chain to nil and do nothing. Simultaneously the write API (setSessionHidden, renameSession, exportSession, setFavorite, recordSessionAccess) ships with zero app callers.

Design in three surgical pieces:

(1) NEW FILE macos/Engram/Views/SessionActionHandlers.swift — a small @MainActor struct SessionActionHandlers that owns ONLY the side-effecting service calls so the two browse pages reuse instead of duplicate. It does NOT own any sheet-presentation state: resumeTarget/replayTarget/renameTarget remain page @State (the handler never presents a sheet). It takes the EngramServiceClient plus a reload closure and an onStatus closure (transient banner text). Exposes: copyResumeCommand(_:) (mirrors HomeView.copyResumeCommand: serviceClient.resumeCommand -> TodayResumeCommand.copyableClipboardItem -> NSPasteboard + status), handoff(_:) (mirrors SessionDetailView.performHandoff: serviceClient.handoff(EngramServiceHandoffRequest(cwd:sessionId:format:'markdown')) + NSPasteboard + status toast), setHidden(_:hidden:) then reload, rename(_:to:) -> renameSession(name: normalizedName(to)) then reload, export(_:format:) -> exportSession then NSWorkspace.shared.activateFileViewerSelecting([URL(fileURLWithPath: response.outputPath)]) + status, setFavorite(_:favorite:) + status, recordAccess(_:) fire-and-forget. A pure static normalizedName(_:) maps empty/whitespace -> nil, else trimmed. All async work runs in Task; thrown errors route to onStatus. ~110 lines.

(2) EXTEND ExpandableSessionCard (and CompactChildRow): add optional closures onHide/onRename/onExportMarkdown/onExportJSON/onToggleFavorite and a flag isHidden=false (defaulted). isFavorite is intentionally NOT added — browse pages do not load per-session favorite state in this WP (the star glyph + favorites list/filter is WP02), so the favorite menu item uses a fixed 'Favorite' label and onToggleFavorite always toggles to true. The existing 4 items stay; after them add Divider() + Favorite + Rename… + Export submenu (Markdown/JSON) + Hide/Unhide. Each new Button renders only when its closure is non-nil, so SessionDetailView's CompactChildRow usages (which pass none) are unaffected. New closures pass down to confirmed/suggested child rows.

(3) WIRE both browse pages (SessionsPageView AND TimelinePageView — WP01 owns the session-action wiring in BOTH, see outOfScopeNotes for the WP10 boundary): add @State resumeTarget/replayTarget/renameTarget: Session? and actionStatus: String?. Build a SessionActionHandlers from serviceClient/loadData/{ actionStatus = $0 }. Pass onResume (sets resumeTarget + handlers.recordAccess), onCopyResumeCommand/onHandoff, onReplay (sets replayTarget), onHide/onRename (sets renameTarget)/onExportMarkdown/onExportJSON/onToggleFavorite, and isHidden (session.hiddenAt != nil) into ExpandableSessionCard. Call handlers.recordAccess(session) in the existing onTap. Host .sheet(item:$resumeTarget){ ResumeDialog(session:$0) }, .sheet(item:$replayTarget){ SessionReplayView(sessionId:$0.id).frame(minWidth:600,minHeight:450) }, and a small inline rename TextField sheet on $renameTarget. Render actionStatus via AlertBanner when non-nil. Session already conforms to Identifiable (Session.swift:6) with id: String, so .sheet(item:) binds directly — no extension is added.

This is pure wiring; every called method is confirmed below. Favorites LIST/filter (a Favorites screen or filter pill) and the per-card favorite/star indicator are deliberately NOT built — they touch Screen.swift and per-session favorite-state loading, split to WP02. This WP only makes favoriting reachable + gives toast feedback.
- **Changes:**
  - `create` `macos/Engram/Views/SessionActionHandlers.swift` — New @MainActor struct SessionActionHandlers holding serviceClient + reload + onStatus. Side-effecting service calls ONLY (no sheet-presentation state). Methods: copyResumeCommand(_:) (resumeCommand -> TodayResumeCommand.copyableClipboardItem -> clipboard -> status, mirrors HomeView); handoff(_:) (serviceClient.handoff(EngramServiceHandoffRequest(cwd:sessionId:format:'markdown')) + clipboard + status, mirrors SessionDetailView.performHandoff); setHidden(_:hidden:) -> setSessionHidden then reload; rename(_:to:) -> renameSession(name: normalizedName(to)) then reload; export(_:format:) -> exportSession then NSWorkspace.shared.activateFileViewerSelecting + status; setFavorite(_:favorite:) + status; recordAccess(_:) fire-and-forget. Pure static normalizedName(_:) for trim/empty->nil. All async in Task; errors -> onStatus. ~110 lines.
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Components/ExpandableSessionCard.swift` — Add optional onHide/onRename/onExportMarkdown/onExportJSON/onToggleFavorite closures and an isHidden=false flag to ExpandableSessionCard and CompactChildRow (no isFavorite flag — see outOfScopeNotes). Extend both contextMenu builders: after existing Resume/Copy/Handoff/Replay add Divider() + Button('Favorite') + Button('Rename…') + Menu('Export'){Markdown/JSON} + Button(isHidden ? 'Unhide' : 'Hide'), each gated on its closure being non-nil. Pass the new closures into the confirmed/suggested CompactChildRow instances.
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/Pages/SessionsPageView.swift` — Add @State resumeTarget/replayTarget/renameTarget: Session? and actionStatus: String?. Build SessionActionHandlers(serviceClient:reload:onStatus:). Pass onResume(sets resumeTarget + handlers.recordAccess)/onCopyResumeCommand/onHandoff/onReplay(sets replayTarget)/onHide/onRename(sets renameTarget)/onExportMarkdown/onExportJSON/onToggleFavorite + isHidden(session.hiddenAt != nil) into ExpandableSessionCard; call handlers.recordAccess in onTap. Host .sheet(item:$resumeTarget){ResumeDialog}, .sheet(item:$replayTarget){SessionReplayView}, inline rename TextField sheet on $renameTarget. Show actionStatus AlertBanner.
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/Pages/TimelinePageView.swift` — Same session-action wiring as SessionsPageView (WP01 owns this file's session-action wiring; WP10 must not touch it — see outOfScopeNotes): action @State, SessionActionHandlers, pass the new closures + isHidden into ExpandableSessionCard, call handlers.recordAccess in onTap, host resume/replay/rename sheets + status banner.
  - `create` `macos/EngramTests/SessionActionsTests.swift` — New XCTest reusing the RecordingServiceTransport actor + Self.payload helper pattern from EngramServiceClientTests. (1) Drive EngramServiceClient via a RecordingServiceTransport whose handler asserts command == setSessionHidden / renameSession / exportSession / setFavorite / recordSessionAccess and decodes each PAYLOAD field only (no capabilityToken assertion); void commands return {} and exportSession returns canned JSON decoding outputPath/format/messageCount; assert transport.sent command order. (2) Pure test of SessionActionHandlers.normalizedName: ''/whitespace -> nil, trimmed otherwise.
- **APIs used:**
  - `EngramServiceClient.setSessionHidden(sessionId:hidden:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func setSessionHidden(sessionId: String, hidden: Bool) async throws — sends command "setSessionHidden", payload EngramServiceSessionHiddenRequest` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClient.renameSession(sessionId:name:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func renameSession(sessionId: String, name: String?) async throws — sends "renameSession", payload EngramServiceRenameSessionRequest(sessionId,name:String?)` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClient.exportSession(_:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func exportSession(_ request: EngramServiceExportSessionRequest) async throws -> EngramServiceExportSessionResponse — sends "exportSession"` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClient.setFavorite(sessionId:favorite:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func setFavorite(sessionId: String, favorite: Bool) async throws — sends "setFavorite", payload EngramServiceFavoriteRequest` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClient.recordSessionAccess(sessionId:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func recordSessionAccess(sessionId: String) async throws — sends "recordSessionAccess", payload EngramServiceSessionAccessRequest` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClient.resumeCommand(sessionId:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func resumeCommand(sessionId: String) async throws -> EngramServiceResumeCommandResponse` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClient.handoff(_:)` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceClient.swift) `func handoff(_ request: EngramServiceHandoffRequest) async throws -> EngramServiceHandoffResponse` ✓
  - `EngramServiceExportSessionRequest` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift) `struct { let id: String; let format: String; let outputHome: String? (output_home); let actor: String? }` ✓
  - `EngramServiceExportSessionResponse` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift) `struct { let outputPath: String; let format: String; let messageCount: Int }` ✓
  - `EngramServiceHandoffRequest` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift) `struct { let cwd: String; let sessionId: String; let format: String? } (init used as (cwd:sessionId:format:))` ✓
  - `EngramServiceHandoffResponse` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift) `struct { let brief: String; let sessionCount: Int }` ✓
  - `EngramServiceFavoriteRequest / SessionHiddenRequest / RenameSessionRequest / SessionAccessRequest` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift) `Favorite{sessionId,favorite:Bool}; Hidden{sessionId,hidden:Bool}; Rename{sessionId,name:String?}; Access{sessionId} — used to decode/assert payload fields in the test` ✓
  - `ExpandableSessionCard / CompactChildRow` (macos/Engram/Components/ExpandableSessionCard.swift) `ExpandableSessionCard has onResume/onCopyResumeCommand/onHandoff/onReplay/onConfirmSuggestion/onDismissSuggestion optional closures; parent contextMenu :116-129; CompactChildRow contextMenu :342-355` ✓
  - `Session` (macos/Engram/Models/Session.swift) `struct Session: FetchableRecord, Decodable, Identifiable (line 6); let id: String; let cwd: String; let hiddenAt: String?; let customName: String?; var displayTitle (customName ?? generatedTitle ?? …)` ✓
  - `SessionDetailView.performHandoff (reference)` (macos/Engram/Views/SessionDetailView.swift) `:704 performHandoff() = serviceClient.handoff(EngramServiceHandoffRequest(cwd:session.cwd, sessionId:session.id, format:"markdown")) + NSPasteboard + handoffStatus toast` ✓
  - `HomeView.copyResumeCommand (reference)` (macos/Engram/Views/Pages/HomeView.swift) `:305 serviceClient.resumeCommand -> TodayResumeCommand.copyableClipboardItem(from:) -> NSPasteboard.setString(item.text) + alertMessage = item.message` ✓
  - `ResumeDialog / SessionReplayView` (macos/Engram/Views/Resume/ResumeDialog.swift, macos/Engram/Views/Replay/SessionReplayView.swift) `ResumeDialog(session: Session) (init line 31); SessionReplayView { let sessionId: String } — both already hosted as sheets in SessionDetailView:460-466` ✓
  - `AlertBanner` (macos/Engram/Components/AlertBanner.swift) `struct AlertBanner: View (message-based banner already used in SessionsPageView and HomeView)` ✓
  - `RecordingServiceTransport + Self.payload (test harness)` (macos/EngramTests/EngramServiceClientTests.swift) `:332 private actor RecordingServiceTransport: EngramServiceTransport (records requests/sent, returns canned envelopes); :326 private static func payload<T:Decodable>(_:as:) decodes request.payload — reused for SessionActionsTests` ✓
- **UX behavior:** Context menu (right-click a session card on Sessions or Timeline, parent row AND each agent child row):
- Resume… : sets resumeTarget which presents ResumeDialog as a .sheet(item:) (the exact dialog used from SessionDetailView). On present, handlers.recordAccess fires fire-and-forget. ResumeDialog surfaces its own inline CLI-detection error — unchanged.
- Copy Resume Command : calls resumeCommand, copies to clipboard, shows a success banner (item.message); failure shows 'Failed to copy resume command'. Mirrors HomeView.
- Handoff : calls handoff(cwd: session.cwd, sessionId, format 'markdown'), copies brief, shows 'Handoff copied! (N sessions)' toast; failure 'Handoff failed: <error>'. Mirrors SessionDetailView.
- Replay : sets replayTarget which presents SessionReplayView as a .sheet(item:).
- Favorite : calls setFavorite(favorite: true). Fixed label 'Favorite' (browse pages do not load per-session favorite state in this WP, so there is no Unfavorite label and no star glyph — that is WP02). Success/failure shows a brief banner (no silent failure on this path).
- Rename… : sets renameTarget which presents a small sheet with a TextField prefilled with customName ?? displayTitle and Save/Cancel. Save calls renameSession(name: normalizedName(input)) (trimmed, or nil when cleared/whitespace -> reverts to auto title); sheet dismisses and the list reloads (displayTitle updates). Failure: 'Rename failed' banner.
- Export ▸ Markdown / JSON : calls exportSession(format:). Success reveals response.outputPath in Finder via NSWorkspace.shared.activateFileViewerSelecting and shows 'Exported to <filename>'. Failure: 'Export failed: <error>'.
- Hide / Unhide : single item, label 'Unhide' when session.hiddenAt != nil else 'Hide'. Calls setSessionHidden then reload(). With 'Show hidden sessions' OFF, hiding removes the row on reload (the toggle finally has a producer); with it ON the row stays and its label flips after reload.

States/edges:
- Service busy/unavailable: any throwing call routes to onStatus -> transient AlertBanner; removes the 'nothing happened' ambiguity.
- Missing cwd: handoff/resume tolerate nil-equivalent cwd (cwd is non-optional on Session; ResumeDialog shows its own error if needed) — no new handling.
- Rapid taps: rename/export/hide are single idempotent commands; the rename sheet dismisses on save.
- HomeView and SessionDetailView are NOT modified; their menus keep working because the new card closures are optional and gated on non-nil.
- **Acceptance:**
  - Right-clicking a session on the Sessions page and choosing Resume presents ResumeDialog (previously no-op); Copy Resume Command writes the clipboard; Handoff copies a brief; Replay opens the replay sheet.
  - The same four actions work from the Timeline page parent rows and from agent child rows in both pages.
  - Hide on a visible session calls setSessionHidden(hidden:true); with 'Show hidden sessions' off the row leaves the list after reload; the menu label reads 'Unhide' for an already-hidden session and restores it.
  - Rename… opens a sheet; saving a non-empty name calls renameSession with that name and the card title updates after reload; clearing the field calls renameSession(name: nil).
  - Export ▸ Markdown/JSON calls exportSession and reveals the returned outputPath in Finder.
  - Favorite calls setFavorite(favorite:true) and shows a success or failure banner (no silent failure on the browse-page path).
  - Opening or resuming a session calls recordSessionAccess(sessionId:).
  - HomeView and SessionDetailView behavior is unchanged (their cards/menus still work; no new closures required there).
  - SessionActionsTests passes: the new client write commands encode the correct command name + payload fields (no capabilityToken assertion) and round-trip, and SessionActionHandlers.normalizedName maps empty/whitespace -> nil and non-empty -> trimmed.
- **Test plan:** Add macos/EngramTests/SessionActionsTests.swift (XCTest, @testable import Engram), reusing the existing private RecordingServiceTransport actor and the private static Self.payload(_:as:) decode helper pattern from EngramServiceClientTests:
1. testSessionWriteCommandsEncodePayloads — drive EngramServiceClient via a RecordingServiceTransport whose handler switches on request.command and asserts command == setSessionHidden / renameSession / exportSession / setFavorite / recordSessionAccess, decoding each PAYLOAD ONLY (no capabilityToken field assertion — RecordingServiceTransport does not enforce it and the client may attach one): EngramServiceSessionHiddenRequest.hidden; EngramServiceRenameSessionRequest.name asserted both nil and 'Auth refactor'; EngramServiceExportSessionRequest.format 'markdown'/'json'; EngramServiceFavoriteRequest.favorite; EngramServiceSessionAccessRequest.sessionId. Void commands return {} (EmptyServiceResult decodes from {}); exportSession returns canned JSON and the test asserts the decoded response outputPath/format/messageCount. Assert transport.sent command order.
2. testRenameNameNormalization — pure SessionActionHandlers.normalizedName(_:): '' -> nil, '   ' -> nil, '  Auth refactor  ' -> 'Auth refactor', 'x' -> 'x'.
These cover the production write paths per the test-coverage rule without a SwiftUI host; the closure plumbing is exercised structurally (closures call the tested client methods).
- **Risks:** Low. (1) Session ALREADY conforms to Identifiable (Session.swift:6) with id: String — the prior 'add extension if missing' contingency is dropped; do NOT add an extension (a duplicate conformance would not compile). Bind .sheet(item:) directly. (2) Three separate Session? sheet items on one view is fine; only one action runs at a time so simultaneous-sheet conflicts don't arise. (3) ExpandableSessionCard is NOT used by HomeView (it uses TodaySessionRow) — only SessionsPageView/TimelinePageView/SessionDetailView child rows construct it; new optional closures default nil so SessionDetailView's CompactChildRow usage is unaffected. (4) NSWorkspace.shared.activateFileViewerSelecting on a file in ~/.engram/exports works for the current user (app is unsandboxed per entitlements) — no TCC issue. (5) FILE-OWNERSHIP: TimelinePageView.swift is claimed by both WP01 and WP10 in the original backlog; this WP takes sole ownership of its session-action wiring. WP10 must not edit TimelinePageView's session-action wiring or a second merge clobbers the first (see outOfScopeNotes).
- **Out of scope:** FILE-CONFLICT RESOLUTION (TimelinePageView.swift): WP01 owns ALL session-action wiring for both SessionsPageView and TimelinePageView. WP10 (which listed TimelinePageView alongside ActivityView/ReposView/WorkGraphView) must drop TimelinePageView's session-action wiring from its scope; if WP10 needs an unrelated TimelinePageView change it must rebase onto WP01's edits, not re-add session-action closures. This boundary must be honored before either WP merges.

FAVORITES (partial — not fully closed): This WP makes favoriting REACHABLE from the card menu with toast feedback, but does NOT build a Favorites LIST/filter/screen, does NOT add a per-card star glyph, and does NOT load per-session favorite state — so there is no 'Unfavorite' label or toggle-to-false on the browse cards (the menu always calls setFavorite(favorite:true)). That visual indicator + filter + Screen.swift surface is WP02. Consequently sessions-browse-5 ('show a star on the card') is NOT claimed here, and xc-capability-matrix-2 ('nowhere to VIEW favorites') is NOT claimed here.

session-actions-6 (NOT fully closed — removed from findingsCovered): its evidence targets SessionDetailView.swift:177-179 (favorite toggle catch only logs), which is WP03-owned. WP01 only adds favorite-with-banner on the new browse-page call sites; it does not touch the SessionDetailView log-only catch. Coordinate the SessionDetailView one-line fix with WP03; do not claim session-actions-6 as closed by WP01.

session-actions-5 (HALF closed — removed from findingsCovered; only the recordSessionAccess half is wired): the finding has two parts — (1) recordSessionAccess is never called, and (2) the accessedDesc/accessedAsc sort is not exposed in any sort picker. WP01 wires recordSessionAccess (part 1, so the data populates) but does NOT add an accessed sort option to the TimelinePageView/SessionsPageView pickers. Part 2 is DEFERRED to the favorites/sort UI WP (WP02). xc-capability-matrix-9 (purely 'recordSessionAccess is never called') IS fully closed by this wiring and remains in findingsCovered.

Also out of scope: bulk hideEmptySessions wiring (hygiene-3), Hygiene-page Fix actions (hygiene-2), undo-for-hide (hygiene-6) — separate Hygiene WPs. Does NOT modify SessionDetailView or HomeView (their Resume/Handoff/Replay/Favorite already work) beyond sharing the ExpandableSessionCard whose new closures are optional. Does NOT modify any service command, schema, or DTO. The SessionActionHandlers struct holds side-effecting service calls ONLY — it does not own resume/replay/rename sheet-presentation state (that stays as page @State).

### WP02 — Favorites read surface (close write-only dead-end) + shared first-load skeleton convention

- **Disposition:** wire-up  ·  **Critique:** needs-revision (revised)
- **Closes:** xc-capability-matrix-1 (CLOSED IN WP02 — favorites half only): adds a screen that READS Database.listFavorites(), making starred sessions browsable. The insight create/delete UI (saveInsight/deleteInsight/getInsights) half stays out of scope — separate Memory-page feature, see outOfScopeNotes., sessions-browse-2 (DESIGNED here, NOT CLOSED by WP02 — HARD DEPENDENCY on WP01): listSessions already supports offset (Database.swift:179-180,196-197, confirmed). The load-more trigger edits SessionsPageView.swift which is WP01-owned. WP02 ships only the listSessions(offset:) regression test that backs the contract; WP01 wires the UI. Orchestrator must NOT mark this done when WP02 lands., sessions-browse-6 (DESIGNED here, NOT CLOSED by WP02 — HARD DEPENDENCY on WP01): the first-load SkeletonRow convention is defined here and applied to FavoritesPageView, but the Sessions-list first-load fix is a SessionsPageView.swift edit owned by WP01. WP02 closes this finding only for the new page, not for Sessions., xc-states-3 (PARTIALLY addressed in WP02): the no-zeroed-KPI convention is applied to FavoritesPageView (the page WP02 creates). The finding spans many KPI/metric pages; HomeView already complies, SessionsPageView is WP01's to fix, and Activity/other KPI pages are out of WP02 scope. WP02 fixes this on FavoritesPageView only and specifies it for WP01.
- **Goal:** Give favorites a read surface by adding a Favorites screen that reads the already-existing Database.listFavorites(), closing the write-only dead-end (sessions can be starred but never browsed). Establish the shared first-load skeleton convention (SkeletonRow on first paint, no zeroed-KPI flash) and apply it to the new FavoritesPageView. NOTE: this WP's own diff closes only the favorites half of xc-capability-matrix-1; the Sessions-list pagination/loading findings (sessions-browse-2, sessions-browse-6) and the broad xc-states-3 are DESIGNED here but their fixes land in WP01 (SessionsPageView.swift) — see findingsCovered and outOfScopeNotes for the hard-dependency framing.
- **Approach:** Favorites are write-only because nothing reads Database.listFavorites() (Database.swift:627, confirmed: zero-arg, throws -> [Session], guards tableExists(\"favorites\"), filters s.hidden_at IS NULL, ORDER BY f.created_at DESC). The honest completion is a read surface: a new Screen case + a page.\n\n1) Screen.swift (WP02-owned): add `case favorites` to the enum; add its title/localizedTitle (\"Favorites\"), icon (\"star\"), and insert `.favorites` into Section.monitor.screens right after `.sessions` (Screen.swift:102). SidebarView renders purely from Screen.Section.allCases→section.screens (confirmed), so the sidebar entry appears with NO SidebarView body edit.\n\n2) MainWindowView.pageView(for:) — CROSS-WP, WP18-OWNED (corrected from the prior draft which mis-attributed this to WP01). pageView(for:) is an exhaustive `switch screen` (MainWindowView.swift:80-114, confirmed — 16 cases, no default). Adding `case favorites` to Screen makes this switch non-exhaustive, so the entire app fails to compile until `case .favorites: FavoritesPageView()` is added there. This one-line router case is the only cross-WP coupling and MUST be coordinated with WP18 (the MainWindowView owner). WP02 does NOT own MainWindowView.swift; it lists the required line as a coordination item, not an edit it performs unilaterally.\n\n3) FavoritesPageView.swift (new, WP02-owned, auto-included by xcodegen directory sources): a minimal read-only list mirroring SessionsPageView's confirmed structure but trimmed. No time/source filters (favorites is a curated set), NO KPI/count card (cut per critique — a header count adds little for an inherently-small curated set and risks its own zero-flash; render the list + EmptyState only). Loads via `Task.detached { try db.listFavorites() }.value` inside a private `loadData() async`, called from `.task` — exactly SessionsPageView.loadData's pattern (confirmed lines 104-138; DatabaseManager read methods are plain sync funcs on a `final class @unchecked Sendable`, no `nonisolated` keyword, called from views via Task.detached{...}.value). Renders each favorite via the existing ExpandableSessionCard/SessionCard row with onTap → NotificationCenter.post(.openSession, SessionBox(session)) — identical to SessionsPageView:73. EmptyState(icon:\"star\") when `favorites.isEmpty && !isLoading`; AlertBanner(message:) on load error.\n\n4) First-load skeleton convention (xc-states-3 / sessions-browse-6, FavoritesPageView only): while `isLoading && favorites.isEmpty`, render ~3-4 SkeletonRow placeholders in the list area instead of a blank gap, mirroring HomeView's first-load pattern. No zeroed KPICards are ever shown (none exist on this page). The SAME convention is specified for WP01 to apply to SessionsPageView (SkeletonRows while `isLoading && sessions.isEmpty`; KPI values as `—`/skeleton until first load).\n\n5) Pagination (sessions-browse-2, DESIGNED for WP01): the load-more trigger (last-row onAppear → offset += 200 and append, or a \"Load more (N remaining)\" footer when sessions.count < totalCount) edits SessionsPageView.swift (WP01-owned). WP02 ships only the listSessions(offset:) disjoint-pages regression test in its own new test file.

Selecting it routes to FavoritesPageView via MainWindowView.pageView(for:).\n\nFavoritesPageView states:\n- First load (isLoading && favorites empty): ~3-4 SkeletonRow placeholders in the list area (mirrors HomeView). KPI cards render `—`/skeleton until first load completes rather than \"0\".
- **Acceptance:**
  - A 'Favorites' entry (star icon) appears in the sidebar MONITOR section under 'Sessions' and navigates to FavoritesPageView.
  - FavoritesPageView lists sessions returned by Database.listFavorites(), most-recently-favorited first, and tapping a row opens that session's transcript via .openSession(SessionBox(session)).
  - With no favorites, FavoritesPageView shows the star EmptyState telling the user how to add favorites; with a load error it shows an AlertBanner and isLoading clears (no infinite skeleton).

  - sessions-browse-2 and sessions-browse-6 are NOT marked closed by WP02 alone — they require WP01's SessionsPageView edits; xc-states-3 is only partially addressed (FavoritesPageView only).

No SwiftUI snapshot harness exists in this repo, so FavoritesPageView rendering is validated by build + the reachability/data tests rather than a UI test (consistent with the repo's data/threading-contract testing approach, not pixels).

### WP03 — Search → transcript handoff + find-in-page correctness (Text mode, scroll-to-match, Return-advances, current-match counter)

- **Disposition:** wire-up  ·  **Critique:** needs-revision (revised)
- **Closes:** search-1, session-detail-transcript-1, session-detail-transcript-2, session-detail-transcript-3, session-detail-transcript-4, session-detail-transcript-6
- **Goal:** When a user opens a session from keyword search, the transcript opens with the find bar primed to that query and scrolled to the first match. Make the transcript find bar behave like a native macOS find bar: Return advances, the query auto-scrolls/auto-selects the first match, the current-match index resets when the query changes, Text-mode rows actually highlight and scroll into view, and a long transcript offers a jump-to-top affordance. This WP OWNS the full search-1 carrier end to end (SessionBox.searchTerm + the MainWindowView .openSession handler/construction site + the SessionDetailView receiver), so the behavior actually fires rather than sitting inert behind a defaulted-nil parameter.
- **Approach:** Transcript-find state and logic live in SessionDetailView.swift (owned) and TranscriptFindBar.swift (owned). The search-1 carrier touches two small extra files — AppNotifications.swift and MainWindowView.swift — which this WP NOW OWNS for the surgical carrier edit (the original design's claim that WP04 owned this carrier was wrong: WP04 owns only SearchPageView/CommandPaletteView, and the .openSession handler + construction site live in MainWindowView, the SessionBox payload in AppNotifications). All fixes are surgical state/wiring changes, no new backend.\n\n(A) search-1 — carry the query, END TO END (this WP owns the whole carrier).\n  (A1) AppNotifications.swift: add `let searchTerm: String?` to `SessionBox` and a second initializer / default-nil param so existing `SessionBox(session)` call sites stay byte-for-byte unchanged. Concretely: `init(_ session: Session, searchTerm: String? = nil)`. Every current producer (popover, palette, parent/child nav) calls `SessionBox(session)` → searchTerm defaults to nil → unchanged.\n  (A2) MainWindowView.swift: (i) add `@State private var pendingSearchTerm: String? = nil`; (ii) in the `.openSession` handler (line 45-50) set `pendingSearchTerm = box.searchTerm` alongside `selectedSession = box.session`; (iii) at the construction site (line 18) pass `searchTerm: pendingSearchTerm` into `SessionDetailView(session:onBack:searchTerm:)`; (iv) clear `pendingSearchTerm = nil` in the existing `.onChange(of: selectedScreen)` reset block (line 40-44) alongside `selectedSession = nil`, so navigating away can't leak a stale term into the next opened session. The actual producer that posts `SessionBox(session, searchTerm: query)` from the search result row lives in SearchPageView.swift, which WP04 owns — that is the ONE remaining cross-WP dependency, and it is a pure additive call-site change (WP04 swaps `SessionBox(session)` for `SessionBox(session, searchTerm: query)`). Until WP04 lands that, every other caller still passes nil and behavior is unchanged; once WP04 lands it, search-1 fires with zero further WP03 change. This is an honest, scoped hand-off of exactly one additive argument, not a claim that the carrier already exists.\n  (A3) SessionDetailView.swift: add `var searchTerm: String? = nil`. In the per-session `.task(id: session.id)` reset block, replace the unconditional `searchText = \"\"` priming (line 428) with `searchText = searchTerm ?? \"\"`, and set `showFind = (searchTerm?.isEmpty == false)`. When `searchTerm` is nil, this is `searchText = \"\"` and `showFind = false` — identical to today.\n\n(C) session-detail-transcript-3 + -4 — auto-select first match on query, reset on query change. Add `.onChange(of: searchText) { _, _ in currentMatchIndex = -1; scrollTarget = nil }` so a new/edited query restarts navigation from the top (closes -4's stale-position decoupling). Then in `updateMatchIndicesDebounced()`, the empty-query early return at line 143 (`matchIndices = []; return`) stays INTACT (an empty query must not auto-scroll); the auto-select block is inserted strictly AFTER `matchIndices = indices` (line 153, post-`Task.isCancelled` guard) so it never reads a stale `matchIndices`: `if currentMatchIndex < 0, let first = indices.first { currentMatchIndex = 0; scrollTarget = displayIndexed[first].id }`. The `currentMatchIndex < 0` guard is what makes this interact deterministically with the onChange reset (onChange sets -1 → scan sets 0) and what stops it fighting an in-progress Prev/Next (if the user already navigated, currentMatchIndex >= 0 so a re-scan from a filter/page change won't yank them back to the first match). Uses the existing live `displayIndexed` snapshot, stays in `navigateFind`'s index space (matchIndices → displayIndexed.id).\n\n(D) session-detail-transcript-2 — Return advances. Add `.onSubmit { onNext() }` to the Find TextField in TranscriptFindBar.swift (the bar already exposes `onNext`/`onPrev`). Shift-Return → onPrev is out of scope (SwiftUI `.onSubmit` carries no modifier; the existing ⌘⇧G shortcut at SessionDetailView.swift:399 already covers reverse).\n\n(B) session-detail-transcript-1 — Text mode highlight + scroll. In the `.text` branch of the transcript (lines 369-372), add `.id(msg.id)` to each `RawMessageRow` and pass `searchText:` into it. Because `IndexedMessage.id == message.id` (IndexedMessage.swift) and `displayIndexed` wraps the SAME ChatMessage instances built from `messages`, the `scrollTarget` UUID that `navigateFind`/auto-select derive from `displayIndexed[idx].id` resolves to a real Text-mode anchor — Prev/Next/Return/auto-scroll work in Text mode with no new index space. Extend `RawMessageRow` with `var searchText: String = \"\"` and render its content `Text` through an in-file `highlight(_:query:)` helper (case-insensitive AttributedString, yellow background / black foreground, same semantics as ColorBarMessageView.highlightedText but self-contained since ColorBarMessageView.swift is not owned by this WP). The default `searchText = \"\"` keeps Text mode unchanged when no query is active.\n\n(E) session-detail-transcript-6 — jump-to-top. Add a single small floating up-chevron Button as `.overlay(alignment: .bottomTrailing)` on the transcript ScrollView (inside the existing `ScrollViewReader`, owned region, lines 359-385), shown only when `displayIndexed.count > 1`, wired to `scrollTarget = displayIndexed.first?.id` (reuses the existing proxy + `onChange(of: scrollTarget)` path at line 380-384; the existing `.center` anchor scrolls the first row fully into view). Kept to a ~8-line overlay per the minimal-surface guidance. No TranscriptToolbar edit.\n\nDROPPED FROM THE ORIGINAL DESIGN (per critique, to stay minimal):\n  - The Text-mode-only orange `isCurrentMatch` accent background on RawMessageRow is CUT. It gold-plated one view mode (Text) while the default Session mode got no distinct color, creating asymmetric current-match treatment for a Low finding. Current-match is conveyed in BOTH modes by the N/M counter (already in TranscriptFindBar) + auto-scroll-to-center (existing `.center` anchor). session-detail-transcript-5 is therefore NOT in this WP's closed set — see outOfScopeNotes.\n  - search-4 (recent-query chips) and session-detail-transcript-7 (rich-rendering loss during search) are removed from findingsCovered entirely: this WP makes zero code change for either, so neither can be claimed closed. Both are documented in outOfScopeNotes as deferred to the owning WP.
- **Changes:**
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/AppNotifications.swift` — Add `let searchTerm: String?` to `SessionBox` and change its initializer to `init(_ session: Session, searchTerm: String? = nil) { self.session = session; self.searchTerm = searchTerm }`. Default-nil keeps every existing `SessionBox(session)` call site unchanged.
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/MainWindowView.swift` — Add `@State private var pendingSearchTerm: String? = nil`. In the `.openSession` handler, set `pendingSearchTerm = box.searchTerm` alongside `selectedSession = box.session`. At the construction site (line 18), pass `searchTerm: pendingSearchTerm` into SessionDetailView. In the existing `.onChange(of: selectedScreen)` reset (line 40-44), also clear `pendingSearchTerm = nil`.
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/SessionDetailView.swift` — Add `var searchTerm: String? = nil` property. In `.task(id: session.id)`, replace `searchText = ""` (line 428) with `searchText = searchTerm ?? ""` and set `showFind = (searchTerm?.isEmpty == false)`. Add `.onChange(of: searchText) { _, _ in currentMatchIndex = -1; scrollTarget = nil }`. In `updateMatchIndicesDebounced()`, AFTER `matchIndices = indices` (line 153), insert auto-select-first guarded by `currentMatchIndex < 0`: `if currentMatchIndex < 0, let first = indices.first { currentMatchIndex = 0; scrollTarget = displayIndexed[first].id }` (empty-query early return at line 143 left intact). In the `.text` ForEach (line 369-372), add `.id(msg.id)` and pass `searchText: searchText` into RawMessageRow. Add an `.overlay(alignment: .bottomTrailing)` scroll-to-top chevron button on the transcript ScrollView (inside the ScrollViewReader), shown when `displayIndexed.count > 1`, wired to `scrollTarget = displayIndexed.first?.id`. Extend RawMessageRow with `var searchText: String = ""` and an in-file case-insensitive `highlight(_:query:) -> AttributedString` helper used to render `message.content`.
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/Transcript/TranscriptFindBar.swift` — Add `.onSubmit { onNext() }` to the Find TextField so Return advances to the next match (native macOS find-bar idiom).
  - `create` `macos/EngramTests/TranscriptFindTests.swift` — New XCTestCase: (1) pure-logic tests over the existing static helpers (nextFindMatchIndex wrap 0→1→2→0, displayedFindMatchIndex(current:-1,count:n)==0 clamp) locking the auto-select-first + restart-from-top index math; (2) #filePath source-contract assertions (normalized/loose substring per critique) for: SessionBox carries searchTerm; MainWindowView passes searchTerm: and clears pendingSearchTerm; SessionDetailView seeds `searchText = searchTerm`, has `.onChange(of: searchText)` setting `currentMatchIndex = -1`, has the auto-select guarded by `currentMatchIndex < 0`; .text ForEach carries `.id(msg.id)` + `RawMessageRow(` with `searchText:`; TranscriptFindBar has `.onSubmit` calling `onNext`.
- **APIs used:**
  - `SessionBox` (macos/Engram/AppNotifications.swift) `final class SessionBox { let session: Session; init(_ session: Session) { self.session = session } } — NO searchTerm field today; this WP adds `let searchTerm: String?` + `init(_:searchTerm:String?=nil)`` ✓
  - `.openSession` (macos/Engram/AppNotifications.swift) `static let openSession = Notification.Name("com.engram.openSession")` ✓
  - `MainWindowView .openSession handler + construction site` (macos/Engram/Views/MainWindowView.swift) `line 18: SessionDetailView(session: session, onBack: { selectedSession = nil }); line 45-50: .onReceive(... .openSession) { if let box = notification.object as? SessionBox { pendingNavigationId = nil; selectedSession = box.session } }; line 40-44: .onChange(of: selectedScreen){ pendingNavigationId = nil; selectedSession = nil } — handler reads ONLY box.session today; this WP (owns this file) adds pendingSearchTerm` ✓
  - `SessionDetailView` (macos/Engram/Views/SessionDetailView.swift) `struct SessionDetailView: View { let session: Session; var onBack: (() -> Void)? = nil; @State searchText="" (51); @State showFind=false (50); @State currentMatchIndex:Int = -1 (52); @State scrollTarget: UUID? = nil (57) }` ✓
  - `SessionDetailView.updateMatchIndicesDebounced` (macos/Engram/Views/SessionDetailView.swift) `private func updateMatchIndicesDebounced() async (141-154): empty-query early return `matchIndices = []; return` (143); 200ms sleep; off-main scan; `matchIndices = indices` (153) after final Task.isCancelled guard (152).   - `SessionDetailView.displayedFindMatchIndex / nextFindMatchIndex` (macos/Engram/Views/SessionDetailView.swift) `static func nextFindMatchIndex(current:direction:count:)->Int? (680-682) wraps via nextNavPosition; static func displayedFindMatchIndex(current:count:)->Int? (684-687) returns min(max(current,0),count-1) — clamps -1→0` ✓
