- **UX behavior:** Layout (top→bottom inside the existing ScrollView):
- AlertBanner on loadError (unchanged).
- KPI cards: keep "Agent Sessions" + "Active (7d)". DETERMINISTIC KPI SOURCE: since the main list now switches from subAgent sessions to top-level parents, the previous activeCount (distinct agentRoles among agentSessions) becomes meaningless. Both KPI numbers derive from ONE dedicated count-only read of the subagent population: keep `let subagents = db.listSessions(subAgent: true, limit: 200)` solely to feed the KPIs (NOT rendered as the list). "Agent Sessions" = subagents.count; "Active (7d)" = distinct agentRoles among subagents started in the last 7d. This is a single code path feeding both labels; no derived-from-groups sum.
- PENDING SUGGESTIONS section (only rendered when non-empty): SectionHeader(icon:"questionmark.circle", title:"Pending Suggestions") + a count. Each row is an AgentsView-owned row (NOT an ExpandableSessionCard): session title/source + a short "suggested under <parent>" hint, with Confirm / Dismiss buttons and an overflow 'Set parent…'. Confirm → serviceClient.confirmSuggestion → reload; row disappears. Dismiss → guard `if let sp = child.suggestedParentId` then serviceClient.dismissSuggestion(sessionId:, suggestedParentId: sp) → reload; row disappears. 'Set parent…' → presents LinkParentPicker for that child. While a row's action is in-flight, that row's buttons are .disabled and show a small ProgressView; on error, set loadError (AlertBanner) and leave the row. accessibilityIdentifier 'agents_pendingList' on the section.
- AGENT GROUPS section: SectionHeader(icon:"cpu", title:"Agent Sessions"). For each top-level parent with children/suggestions, an ExpandableSessionCard. Tapping the parent posts .openSession (unchanged); expanding loads children (card-owned); Confirm/Dismiss INSIDE the card hit the same helpers via onConfirmSuggestion/onDismissSuggestion. NO Set-parent affordance is added to these cards (the card has no such hook and editing it is out of WP07 scope). accessibilityIdentifier 'agents_list' preserved on the group list.
- EMPTY STATE: when BOTH sections are empty and !isLoading, keep EmptyState(icon:"cpu", title:"No agent sessions", …) with accessibilityIdentifier 'agents_emptyState'.
- LOADING: isLoading starts true; first load shows KPI chrome; add a ProgressView in the list area while isLoading && both sections empty.

LinkParentPicker sheet: title "Set parent"; a search TextField filtering candidate parents by title/project; a scrollable single-select list (excludes the child's own id); Cancel + Link buttons. Link disabled until a parent is selected. On Link: show ProgressView, call setParentSession; if response.ok dismiss + invoke onLinked (parent reloads); if !ok or thrown, show the error string inline (red caption) and keep the sheet open. Self-link prevented by excluding child's id; service also validates depth/self-link (belt-and-suspenders).

EDGE CASES: missing/empty service response error → inline message, no crash. Service busy/timeout → caught; surfaced via AlertBanner (groups/inbox) or inline (picker); page stays usable. A child whose suggestedParentId became nil between load and Dismiss → the `if let sp` guard skips the call (mirrors SessionsPageView). Rapid double-tap on Confirm/Dismiss → row buttons disabled while in-flight.
- **Acceptance:**
  - AgentsView renders ExpandableSessionCard (not SessionCard) for agent groups and passes onConfirmSuggestion/onDismissSuggestion wired to serviceClient.confirmSuggestion/dismissSuggestion.
  - A 'Pending Suggestions' section lists every session with non-null suggested_parent_id (via new db.pendingSuggestionSessions) with inline Confirm and Dismiss that reload on success; Dismiss is guarded by `if let suggestedParentId`.
  - A 'Set parent…' affordance ON THE PENDING-SUGGESTION ROWS (AgentsView-owned, NOT inside ExpandableSessionCard) opens LinkParentPicker which calls serviceClient.setParentSession(sessionId:parentId:) — the first and only app UI caller of setParentSession.
  - No Set-parent closure is passed to ExpandableSessionCard and ExpandableSessionCard.swift is NOT edited by this WP (no cross-WP file conflict with WP01).
  - AgentsView uses .task(id: serviceStatusStore.totalSessions) so the list and KPIs refresh live as indexing adds sessions, matching ProjectsView/HomeView.
  - Both KPI numbers ('Agent Sessions', 'Active (7d)') come from a single count-only db.listSessions(subAgent:true) read; no derived-from-groups sum and no reuse of the old activeCount over the new parent list.
  - db.pendingSuggestionSessions returns only sessions with suggested_parent_id set AND parent_session_id NULL, excludes hidden unless includeHidden, ordered start_time DESC, capped by limit.
  - linkSessions is explicitly NOT wired (directory re-association, not a parent link); xc-capability-matrix-6's linkSessions limb is documented as deferred/out-of-scope, so the finding is reported as PARTIALLY closed (setParentSession limb only).
  - Empty/loading/error states: ProgressView on first load, EmptyState when no groups and no suggestions, AlertBanner/inline error on failure.
  - Existing accessibility identifiers (agents_container, agents_emptyState, agents_list) preserved; new identifiers added for the pending list and the set-parent affordance.
  - Tests do NOT call DatabaseManagerTests.setParentLinks (private); links are set via an inline DatabaseQueue.write UPDATE. xcodegen not required (new file under macos/Engram/Views/Agents auto-included); project builds.
- **Test plan:** Create macos/EngramTests/AgentsViewTests.swift with two kinds of tests:

1) DB-backed (real DatabaseManager + temp sqlite, mirroring DatabaseManagerTests setUp): create the table via the file-scope global createSessionsTable(at:); insert parent + suggested-child + confirmed-child + an unrelated top-level session via the file-scope global insertTestSession(at:...). SET LINKS BY INLINE WRITE (do NOT call DatabaseManagerTests.setParentLinks — it is private to that class): open a DatabaseQueue on the temp path and run `try queue.write { db in try db.execute(sql: "UPDATE sessions SET suggested_parent_id = ? WHERE id = ?", arguments: ["parent", "sug"]); try db.execute(sql: "UPDATE sessions SET parent_session_id = ? WHERE id = ?", arguments: ["parent", "conf"]) }`. Then construct DatabaseManager on the same path. Assert db.pendingSuggestionSessions().map(\\.id) == ["sug"] (excludes the confirmed child and the unrelated session). Assert a hidden suggested child (UPDATE … SET hidden_at = …) is excluded by default and included when includeHidden:true. Assert the LIMIT is honored. (This is the production read-path behavior change requiring a test per the coverage rule.)

Assert ExpandableSessionCard.swift is unchanged by checking it still contains no 'onSetParent' symbol (proves no cross-WP edit). Assert LinkParentPicker.swift contains 'setParentSession' and reads candidates off-main ('Task.detached').

Optionally exercise the setParentSession success/error branches via MockEngramServiceClient.setParentSessionResult, following EngramServiceClientTests usage of the mock results.
- **Risks:** Database.swift ownership: this WP adds ONE read method (pendingSuggestionSessions) to a shared file not in WP07's owned-files map. Risk is low (read-only, nonisolated via readInBackground, no pre-existing pendingSuggestionSessions symbol, no edits to existing methods, placed adjacent to suggestedChildSessions at ~line 1102) but the edit is outside WP07's stated file scope — this spec explicitly requests a scoped ownership grant for that single addition; if another WP also adds read methods to Database.swift, coordinate placement to avoid a textual collision. KPI semantics: pinned deterministically to a single count-only db.listSessions(subAgent:true) read feeding both labels, so test and code agree; the stale activeCount over the new parent list is removed. Pending-suggestions could be large on a big index; the new query is LIMIT-capped (200), ordered, off-main via readInBackground. ExpandableSessionCard is owned by WP01; this WP consumes only its existing closures and adds NO edit to that file (verified it has no onSetParent), avoiding the hot-file conflict — Set-parent lives only on AgentsView-owned inbox rows. setParentSession depth/self-link validation lives in the service (EngramServiceCommandHandler), so the picker only surfaces EngramServiceLinkResponse.error. Test-helper risk eliminated: links set via inline DatabaseQueue.write, not the private setParentLinks.
- **Out of scope:** PARTIAL CLOSE OF xc-capability-matrix-6: that finding flags BOTH setParentSession AND linkSessions as having no UI. WP07 wires setParentSession (the genuine manual parent link) and deliberately does NOT wire linkSessions — confirmed via EngramServiceClient.swift:157 + EngramServiceLinkSessionsRequest that linkSessions carries {targetDir, actor} and re-associates sessions to a project DIRECTORY (response {created, skipped, errors, targetDir, projectNames}), not a parent/child link. linkSessions therefore does not satisfy the 'Set parent / Link to…' intent and is correctly excluded. Consequently xc-capability-matrix-6 must NOT be reported as fully closed by WP07 alone: the linkSessions limb is deferred/out-of-scope (its real UX, if ever wanted, is project re-association, a different surface). Re-scope the finding to 'setParentSession-only' for WP07, or jointly own the linkSessions limb elsewhere.

ExpandableSessionCard has no onSetParent param and exposes only Resume/Copy/Handoff/Replay in its context menus (ExpandableSessionCard.swift:116-129); delivering Set-parent inside the cards would require editing WP01's file — out of WP07 scope and a file conflict. Set-parent is delivered ONLY on AgentsView-owned pending-suggestion rows, which fully closes agents-grouping-3 / xc-deadends-4 / the setParentSession limb of xc-capability-matrix-6.

The WP brief also listed 'EngramServiceClient.listSessions' — that method does not exist on the client; app session listing is DatabaseManager.listSessions (Database.swift:171), which this WP uses. Does NOT add a new DTO or service command (all four service operations already exist). Test plan does NOT use DatabaseManagerTests.setParentLinks (private to that class) — links set via inline DatabaseQueue.write UPDATE.

### WP08 — Cost/usage: deep-link the pressure notification on tap, give the popover USAGE section an empty/unconfigured state, and honestly defer/hand off the orphan dollar/budget controls

- **Disposition:** mixed  ·  **Critique:** needs-revision (revised)
- **Closes:** usage-cost-3, usage-cost-4
- **Goal:** Close the two findings WP08 can actually close inside its owned files: make the usage-pressure OS notification deep-link to the Sources page on the DEFAULT notification tap (usage-cost-3), and give the popover USAGE section a discoverable empty/unconfigured state (usage-cost-4). For the two findings WP08 cannot close inside its files, do so honestly: precisely document that real per-dollar spend on SourcePulse (usage-cost-1) is NOT a wire-up — no app-reachable query returns dollars — so it is DEFERRED to a backend WP with an exact IPC spec; and that the budget/threshold/long-session controls (usage-cost-2) are a remove-misleading action living in SettingsView.swift, which WP12 owns, so WP08 records it as a BLOCKING handoff to WP12 rather than fabricating a consumer.
- **Approach:** Bookkeeping correction (per critique): WP08's diff only closes usage-cost-3 and usage-cost-4, so findingsCovered is narrowed to exactly those two. usage-cost-1 is DEFERRED (documented backend IPC spec, no app UI in this WP) and usage-cost-2 is a BLOCKING handoff to WP12 (remove-misleading lives in a file WP08 does not own). Both are tracked in outOfScopeNotes, not claimed closed.\n\nGrounding from reading the real code:\n\n(1) usage-cost-1 deferral rationale (unchanged, re-confirmed): the dollar-summing query SUM(c.cost_usd) lives ONLY in macos/EngramMCP/Core/MCPDatabase.swift getCosts(), runs on the MCP process's own DatabaseQueue, and is exposed only via the get_costs MCP tool. EngramServiceClientProtocol (EngramServiceProtocol.swift) has NO cost-dollar method: sources() returns EngramServiceSourceInfo carrying only costedSessionCount (a COUNT), and the only '$' the app sees is provider-reported usage_snapshots cost-share (EngramServiceUsageItem unit==\"$\"), NOT session_costs accumulated spend. So there is no app-reachable query that returns dollars; surfacing real per-dollar spend on SourcePulse requires NEW service plumbing outside this WP's owned files. usage-cost-1 is DEFERRED with an exact backend spec (see outOfScopeNotes); no dollar figure is fabricated from costedSessionCount.\n\n(2) usage-cost-2 handoff rationale: the budget/cost-threshold/long-session keys are written by SettingsView.swift and read back only by SettingsView; UsagePressureNotificationSettings.current() (UsagePressureNotifier.swift:8-14) reads ONLY monitor.enabled + monitor.notifyOnUsagePressure and already ignores the budget/threshold/long-session keys. A real consumer would need accumulated session_costs dollars (unreachable per usage-cost-1) and live session-duration tracking the notifier never receives. The honest fix (remove-misleading) is to remove/gate those controls, but they live in SettingsView.swift which WP12 owns. WP08 therefore makes NO change for usage-cost-2 (the notifier is already honest) and records a BLOCKING dependency on WP12 to remove/gate the named controls; WP08 cannot enforce this and must not mark usage-cost-2 closed if WP12 ships without the removal.\n\n(3) usage-cost-3 is the genuine wire-up I own. UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster (UsagePressureNotifier.swift:56-89) builds a UNMutableNotificationContent with trigger:nil and there is NO UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate anywhere. The load-bearing fix is to install a delegate on the notification center that, on the DEFAULT notification tap (UNNotificationDefaultActionIdentifier), routes to the deep-link. Per the critique I deliberately do NOT add a UNNotificationCategory / 'View Usage' UNNotificationAction / setNotificationCategories registration: that is optional polish beyond the finding's minimum and would create a second, untested code path. The minimum that closes usage-cost-3 is the delegate's didReceive routing on the default tap.\n\nCOLD-WINDOW RACE FIX (correctness, required by critique): the deep-link must post .openWindow synchronously, then post .navigateToScreen on the NEXT run-loop tick inside Task { @MainActor in ... }. Confirmed against real code: MainWindowView.selectedScreen defaults to .home (MainWindowView.swift:5) and its .onReceive(.navigateToScreen) subscriber (MainWindowView.swift:51-56) is attached when SwiftUI mounts the body, which happens on a LATER tick than openWindow()'s synchronous NSHostingController(rootView: MainWindowView()) creation (MenuBarController.swift:252-259). A synchronous .navigateToScreen post would fire before the subscriber attaches and be DROPPED (NotificationCenter does not buffer), leaving a freshly-created window on .home — defeating the deep-link in accessory mode (the common case). The codebase already solves this exact race: handleOpenWindow (MenuBarController.swift:224-231) defers its re-post of .openSession inside Task { @MainActor in ... }. The fix replicates that pattern.\n\nThe tap-routing body is extracted into a small @MainActor method on the poster (e.g. openUsageSurface()) so it is unit-testable without constructing a UNNotification (which is not publicly constructible). The delegate's userNotificationCenter(_:didReceive:withCompletionHandler:) calls openUsageSurface() for the default tap and then completionHandler(). The delegate is assigned center.delegate = self in the poster's init; the poster is retained for the app lifetime via UsagePressureNotifier held by MenuBarController, so taps are delivered.\n\n(4) usage-cost-4 is a wire-up I own in PopoverUsageSection.swift. The whole body is gated on `if !usageData.isEmpty` (line 19) with NO else. I add an else branch rendering the USAGE header plus one muted Button row ('No usage data — set token limits in Settings') whose action posts NotificationCenter.default.post(name: .openSettings) — the same .openSettings path the popover already uses — so the empty state is intentional and discoverable.
- **Changes:**
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/UsagePressureNotifier.swift` — usage-cost-3 wire-up (default-tap deep-link only — NO category/action button). (a) Make UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster conform to NSObject + UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate (it currently has no superclass; UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate requires NSObjectProtocol), and assign center.delegate = self at the end of init(). (b) Add a small @MainActor method `func openUsageSurface()` that posts NotificationCenter.default.post(name: .openWindow) SYNCHRONOUSLY, then posts NotificationCenter.default.post(name: .navigateToScreen, object: Screen.sourcePulse.rawValue) on the NEXT run-loop tick inside `Task { @MainActor in ... }` (mirroring handleOpenWindow at MenuBarController.swift:228-230 to defeat the cold-window race). (c) Implement userNotificationCenter(_:didReceive response:withCompletionHandler:) to, when response.actionIdentifier == UNNotificationDefaultActionIdentifier, call openUsageSurface(); always call completionHandler() at the end. Keep the existing dedupe/severity/authorization logic in UsagePressureNotifier and the content-building in postUsagePressureNotification untouched (content stays category-less, trigger:nil).
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/Usage/PopoverUsageSection.swift` — usage-cost-4 wire-up. Add an `else` branch to the top-level `if !usageData.isEmpty` (line 19) that renders the USAGE header (reusing the existing size 10 semibold .tertiary styling) plus a single muted Button row labeled 'No usage data — set token limits in Settings' whose action posts NotificationCenter.default.post(name: .openSettings). Use .buttonStyle(.plain) and a secondary/tertiary foreground so it reads as a hint, not a primary control. Leave the non-empty branch byte-for-byte unchanged.
  - `edit` `macos/EngramTests/UsagePressureNotifierTests.swift` — Add a focused @MainActor test `testOpenUsageSurfaceDeepLinksToSourcePulse` (REQUIRED — behavior change in a production path). Register a NotificationCenter observer for .openWindow and one for .navigateToScreen; construct a UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster; call its `openUsageSurface()`; await/await-via-expectation the next run-loop tick (the .navigateToScreen post is deferred inside Task { @MainActor in ... }); assert BOTH notifications fire, that .openWindow is observed and that the .navigateToScreen object equals Screen.sourcePulse.rawValue, and assert ORDERING (.openWindow before .navigateToScreen) so the cold-window-race fix cannot regress silently. Use XCTestExpectation(s) fulfilled in the observer closures to handle the next-tick delivery. Keep all existing dedupe/disabled tests unchanged.
- **APIs used:**
  - `UsagePressureNotificationPosting / UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster` (macos/Engram/UsagePressureNotifier.swift) `@MainActor protocol UsagePressureNotificationPosting: AnyObject { func postUsagePressureNotification(_ summary: UsagePressureSummary) }; @MainActor final class UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster: UsagePressureNotificationPosting — init(center: UNUserNotificationCenter = .current()), builds UNMutableNotificationContent with trigger:nil; today has NO superclass and NO delegate (lines 56-89)` ✓
  - `UsagePressureNotificationSettings.current` (macos/Engram/UsagePressureNotifier.swift) `static func current(settings:) reads monitor.enabled + monitor.notifyOnUsagePressure ONLY (lines 8-14); already ignores dailyCostBudget/notifyOnCostThreshold/notifyOnLongSession — no change needed for usage-cost-2` ✓
  - `Notification.Name extensions` (macos/Engram/AppNotifications.swift) `static let openSettings = Notification.Name("com.engram.openSettings"); openWindow = "com.engram.openWindow"; openSession; navigateToScreen = "com.engram.navigateToScreen" (lines 3-8)` ✓
  - `navigateToScreen receiver + default state (cold-window race source)` (macos/Engram/Views/MainWindowView.swift) `@State private var selectedScreen: Screen = .home (line 5); .onReceive(NotificationCenter.default.publisher(for: .navigateToScreen)) { if let raw = obj as? String, let screen = Screen(rawValue: raw) { selectedScreen = screen } } (lines 51-56) — subscriber attaches on body mount, a later tick than openWindow() init` ✓
  - `openWindow() / handleOpenWindow next-tick pattern` (macos/Engram/MenuBarController.swift) `openWindow() builds NSHostingController(rootView: MainWindowView()) synchronously (lines 252-259); handleOpenWindow defers its .openSession re-post inside Task { @MainActor in ... } (lines 224-231) — the exact next-tick pattern openUsageSurface() must replicate; navigateToScreenAction posts .navigateToScreen object: screen.rawValue (lines 446-450)` ✓
  - `Screen.sourcePulse` (macos/Engram/Models/Screen.swift) `enum Screen: String — case sourcePulse (rawValue "sourcePulse", line 16); title/localizedTitle "Sources"; in .workspace section; pageView(for: .sourcePulse) -> SourcePulseView (MainWindowView.swift:98-99)` ✓
  - `PopoverUsageSection` (macos/Engram/Views/Usage/PopoverUsageSection.swift) `struct PopoverUsageSection: View { let usageData: [EngramServiceUsageItem]; @State showAll; body gated on `if !usageData.isEmpty` (line 19) with NO else (closes line 76) }` ✓
  - `EngramServiceUsageItem` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift) `struct { source; metric; value: Double; unit: String?; limit: Double?; resetAt; status } — provider usage; '$' unit is usage-snapshot cost-share, NOT session_costs accumulated spend` ✓
  - `MCPDatabase.getCosts` (macos/EngramMCP/Core/MCPDatabase.swift) `func getCosts(...) — SUM(c.cost_usd) over session_costs; MCP-only, runs on MCP DatabaseQueue, NOT exposed via EngramServiceClientProtocol (basis for usage-cost-1 deferral)` ✓
  - `EngramServiceClientProtocol` (macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceProtocol.swift) `protocol with status/search/sources/usage refresh/etc — NO getCosts / cost / dollar method (basis for usage-cost-1 deferral)` ✓
  - `RecordingUsagePressureNotificationPoster (test seam)` (macos/EngramTests/UsagePressureNotifierTests.swift) `@testable import Engram already used; @MainActor private final class RecordingUsagePressureNotificationPoster: UsagePressureNotificationPosting { var posted: [UsagePressureSummary] } — existing pattern proving the target symbols are test-reachable` ✓
- **UX behavior:** usage-cost-3 (notification deep-link, default tap): Tapping the body of a usage-pressure notification ('Engram usage attention'/'Engram usage critical') opens the main Engram window and navigates to the Sources (SourcePulse) page where per-source usage/cost facts live. States: (a) window already open -> brought to front (via the existing .openWindow handling) and switches to Sources; (b) window closed / app in accessory mode -> .openWindow creates+activates the window, then .navigateToScreen is delivered on the NEXT run-loop tick so the freshly-mounted MainWindowView's .onReceive subscriber is attached and lands the window on Sources (this is the cold-window-race fix; without the next-tick defer the window would stay on the default .home page); (c) authorization not yet granted -> existing behavior unchanged (no notification posts until the user allows). No 'View Usage' action button / expanded-notification action is added (intentionally cut as over-engineering); the deep-link is on the default tap. No change to dedupe/severity behavior.\n\nusage-cost-4 (popover empty state): When usageData is empty (collection hasn't run, no limits configured, or no provider reports usage), the popover now shows the USAGE header and a single muted row 'No usage data — set token limits in Settings'. Tapping it posts .openSettings (the same path the popover already uses) so the user can configure limits. When usageData is non-empty, behavior is identical to today (compact / Show-All metric rows). Edge: the row is a .plain Button with secondary/tertiary color so it reads as a hint, not a primary control.\n\nusage-cost-1 (DEFERRED — not closed by this WP): No new app UI. SourcePulseView keeps its existing 'N costed' count pill and the provider '$X/$Y' usage-limit pill; it does NOT gain a fabricated accumulated-spend figure. A future backend WP adds real total/per-source $ once the service IPC exists.\n\nusage-cost-2 (BLOCKING handoff to WP12 — not closed by this WP): No behavior change in WP08's files. WP08 only confirms UsagePressureNotifier stays honest. WP12 (SettingsView owner) must remove or gate the Daily Budget, Monthly Budget, Long Session, 'Notify on cost threshold', and 'Notify on long session' controls. The 'Notify on usage pressure' toggle and 'Enable background monitor' stay (they ARE consumed by UsagePressureNotifier).
- **Acceptance:**
  - usage-cost-3: UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster installs a UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate (center.delegate = self in init) and its didReceive handler routes the DEFAULT notification tap (UNNotificationDefaultActionIdentifier) to the deep-link, then calls the completion handler.
  - usage-cost-3 (cold-window race): openUsageSurface() posts .openWindow synchronously and posts .navigateToScreen (object == Screen.sourcePulse.rawValue) on the NEXT run-loop tick (inside Task { @MainActor in ... }), so a freshly-created window lands on Sources rather than .home.
  - usage-cost-3: No UNNotificationCategory / 'View Usage' UNNotificationAction / setNotificationCategories registration is added (kept minimal; default-tap routing is the load-bearing path).
  - usage-cost-3: Existing dedupe/severity/disabled-settings behavior of UsagePressureNotifier is unchanged (all current UsagePressureNotifierTests still pass).
  - usage-cost-4: When usageData is empty, PopoverUsageSection renders a USAGE header plus a tappable muted 'No usage data — set token limits in Settings' row that posts .openSettings; when non-empty, output is byte-for-byte the prior behavior.
  - A new Swift test asserts openUsageSurface() posts BOTH .openWindow and .navigateToScreen, that the .navigateToScreen object equals Screen.sourcePulse.rawValue, and that .openWindow is delivered before .navigateToScreen (guarding the next-tick ordering); the full EngramTests suite builds and passes.
  - usage-cost-1 and usage-cost-2 are NOT listed in findingsCovered; usage-cost-1 is documented as DEFERRED with the exact required service-IPC additions, and usage-cost-2 is documented as a BLOCKING dependency on WP12 (must not be marked closed if WP12 ships without removing/gating the named controls).
- **Test plan:** Extend macos/EngramTests/UsagePressureNotifierTests.swift (already uses @testable import Engram and the @MainActor RecordingUsagePressureNotificationPoster pattern). Add `testOpenUsageSurfaceDeepLinksToSourcePulse`: register a NotificationCenter observer for .openWindow and one for .navigateToScreen (capture each notification + a monotonic sequence index, fulfilling an XCTestExpectation per observer to handle the next-tick delivery of .navigateToScreen); construct UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster(); call poster.openUsageSurface(); wait on both expectations; XCTAssert (a) .openWindow fired, (b) .navigateToScreen fired with object as? String == Screen.sourcePulse.rawValue, and (c) the recorded .openWindow sequence index < the .navigateToScreen sequence index (ordering guard for the cold-window-race fix). Remove observers in defer/teardown. The test deliberately exercises the extracted openUsageSurface() seam rather than constructing a UNNotification (not publicly constructible). Keep all existing dedupe/disabled tests unchanged. PopoverUsageSection's empty state is a pure-SwiftUI view change whose only logic is the .openSettings post (mirroring the existing popover pattern); no separate unit test is added for it in this minimal diff.
- **Risks:** UNUserNotificationCenterDelegate requires NSObjectProtocol, so UserNotificationUsagePressurePoster must gain an NSObject superclass — verify this does not break the @MainActor final class declaration or the protocol conformance (NSObject is fine under @MainActor). The delegate must be set before the first notification is delivered and the poster must stay alive for taps — the poster is owned by UsagePressureNotifier held by MenuBarController for the app lifetime, so retention is fine; assigning center.delegate = self in init is the correct seam. The cold-window race is the primary correctness risk and is mitigated by the mandatory next-tick defer of .navigateToScreen (mirroring handleOpenWindow); the new test's ordering assertion guards against silent regression. The deep-link test must avoid constructing a real UNNotification — handled by the extracted openUsageSurface() seam and expectation-based next-tick waiting. BOOKKEEPING: usage-cost-1 (deferred) and usage-cost-2 (WP12 handoff) are NOT closed by this WP's diff; they are intentionally excluded from findingsCovered. usage-cost-2 is a HARD cross-WP dependency: it is only resolved if WP12 actually removes/gates the Daily Budget / Monthly Budget / Long Session / 'Notify on cost threshold' / 'Notify on long session' controls in SettingsView.swift — WP08 cannot enforce this and the orchestrator must not mark usage-cost-2 closed if WP12 ships without that removal.
- **Out of scope:** findingsCovered is intentionally {usage-cost-3, usage-cost-4} only — the two findings WP08's diff actually closes (corrected per critique's header-vs-delivery mismatch).\n\nusage-cost-1 (DEFERRED, not closed): WP08 does NOT build a real per-dollar cost panel on SourcePulse. Reason: the dollar-summing query (SUM(cost_usd)) exists only in MCPDatabase.getCosts (MCP process, separate DatabaseQueue) and there is NO app-reachable service-IPC method returning accumulated spend — EngramServiceSourceInfo carries only costedSessionCount and the app's only '$' values are provider usage_snapshots cost-share, not session_costs. Surfacing real spend requires a NEW costs read in macos/EngramService/Core/EngramServiceReadProvider.swift (SUM(c.cost_usd) grouped by source/total, mirroring sourceCostedCounts), a new command in EngramServiceCommandHandler, a new DTO in EngramServiceModels (e.g. EngramServiceCostSummary { totalUsd; perSource:[String:Double] }), and a method in EngramServiceProtocol + EngramServiceClient — none of which are files WP08 owns. Deferred to a follow-up backend WP. No dollar figure is fabricated from costedSessionCount.\n\nusage-cost-2 (remove-misleading; BLOCKING handoff to WP12, not closed here): the honest fix is to remove/gate the Daily Budget, Monthly Budget, Long Session, 'Notify on cost threshold', and 'Notify on long session' controls, but they live in SettingsView.swift which WP12 owns. WP08 makes NO change for this finding (UsagePressureNotificationSettings.current already reads only monitor.enabled + monitor.notifyOnUsagePressure and ignores the orphan keys). This is an explicit BLOCKING dependency on WP12; the finding must not be marked closed unless WP12 removes/gates the named controls. WP08 does NOT implement a cost-threshold notifier or long-session detector (both need the deferred dollar data and live duration tracking respectively).\n\nMinimality note (per critique): the 'View Usage' UNNotificationAction + UNNotificationCategory + setNotificationCategories registration from the original plan is DROPPED. It is optional polish beyond usage-cost-3's minimum and would add a second untested code path; the load-bearing fix is the delegate's default-tap routing to the deep-link.

### WP09 — Home/Today + popover: make KPI/signal rows actionable, add empty/first-index states, remove dead embedding status

- **Disposition:** mixed  ·  **Critique:** sound (revised)
- **Closes:** home-today-1, home-today-2, home-today-3, home-today-4, home-today-5, settings-ai-3, onboarding-firstrun-2, onboarding-firstrun-3, menubar-popover-1, menubar-popover-2, menubar-popover-3, menubar-popover-4, menubar-popover-5, menubar-popover-6, usage-cost-4-popover
- **Goal:** Turn the Today dashboard and the menu-bar popover from passive readouts into actionable launch points: KPI cards and overflow panels navigate to their full surfaces; the Web UI row opens the browser; the popover surfaces the same live-session count the badge advertises and lets the user open a live session; first-index and zero-data states are distinct and honest; and the never-populated Embeddings status row/dot are removed (UI bindings only) so the UI stops advertising a semantic capability the product does not have.
- **Approach:** All but one finding are pure wire-ups against existing notifications (.navigateToScreen, .openSession, .openWindow, .openSettings) and an existing client method (serviceClient.liveSessions()); the embedding surfaces are a remove-misleading deletion of UI bindings only.

HomeView (Today):
- home-today-1: Wrap the Sessions/Projects/Service KPICards in a Button posting .navigateToScreen — Sessions->.sessions, Projects->.projects, Service->.settings. Leave the "Today" card non-interactive (no single drill-in target). KPICard stays a dumb tile (app-wide convention); navigation lives in HomeView so no other KPICard caller is affected.
- home-today-2: Pass SectionHeader.trailingAction ("See all") into WorkbenchPanel for the three overflow panels, shown only when the loaded count exceeds the display limit. Continue/Follow-ups -> .navigateToScreen(.sessions); Changed Repos -> .navigateToScreen(.projects). WorkbenchPanel gains an optional trailingAction param forwarded to SectionHeader (SectionHeader already supports trailingAction at :9, currently unused).
- home-today-3: Make the "Web UI" ServiceStateRow open http://host:port/ via NSWorkspace.shared.open when a port is present (reuse the exact pattern in MenuBarController.openWebUI at :287-293). ServiceStateRow (the private struct at HomeView.swift:553) gains an optional onTap; only the Web UI row passes it.
- home-today-4 + settings-ai-3 (Home half): REMOVE the Embeddings ServiceStateRow entirely (the "brain" row at HomeView.swift:225-230 bound to serviceStatusStore.embeddingStatus and the "Check Advanced diagnostics" fallback). embeddingStatus is never assigned in production, so the row is permanently the misleading fallback pointing at a non-existent destination. Removing the row (not relabeling) matches the already-removed inert embedding settings controls. Do NOT remove the var embeddingStatus: String? field from EngramServiceStatusStore.swift:37 — that file is shared and its property is exercised by EngramServiceStatusStoreTests; this WP only drops the two UI bindings.
- home-today-5: Route the Changed Repos warning to the Projects page. ChangedRepoRow is currently a single Button(action: onOpen) (HomeView.swift:459-499); add a trailing tappable warning badge (rendered only when projectWarnings[group.id] is non-nil) that posts .navigateToScreen(.projects) instead of opening the transcript, so the signal has a matching action without disturbing the default row-open behavior.
- onboarding-firstrun-2: Add an "indexing in progress" branch to the three workbench panels: when serviceStatusStore.status == .starting, render an "Indexing your sessions…" EmptyState (icon arrow.triangle.2.circlepath) instead of the terminal "No recent work"/"No follow-ups found"/"No project activity" copy. Distinguishes first-index from genuine empty. The existing `.task(id: serviceStatusStore.totalSessions)` reload (HomeView.swift:41) re-runs as counts climb, so panels fill in progressively.

PopoverView (menu-bar popover):
- menubar-popover-1 + -2 + -6: Add a "Live" section at the top of the popover that calls serviceClient.liveSessions() and renders the active/idle entries via LiveSessionCard. The section header count MUST be computed with the IDENTICAL predicate the badge uses — response.sessions.filter { $0.activityLevel == "active" }.count (exactly MenuBarController.updateBadge at :409) — so "●N" in the menu bar maps to a visible "N active" figure and the two cannot diverge. Make LiveSessionCard tappable via a new onOpen closure: when session.sessionId is non-nil, resolve via db.getSession(id:) OFF the main thread (Task.detached { try? db.readInBackground / getSession }, matching the project read rule and the PopoverView.loadData pattern at :206) and then post .openWindow(SessionBox) on the main actor; render non-interactive (no Button, no hover/cursor) when sessionId is nil.
- menubar-popover-3: Add discoverability to the historical timeline rows (timelineRow at :154-181): a .help("Open session") tooltip, a trailing chevron, and an onHover background highlight, plus keep the existing double-click-to-open (.onTapGesture(count: 2)). Single-tap is intentionally NOT added (avoids accidental window-open on a transient popover).
- menubar-popover-4: Add a SINGLE @State Timer (10s) created in .onAppear and invalidated in .onDisappear that re-runs the existing loadData(). Because the live-section fetch is wired into loadData (or a sibling call inside it), this one tick refreshes BOTH the timeline reload AND the live-section fetch — do NOT add a separate live poller cadence or a refresh-token. Mirrors SourcePulseView's single-timer cadence.
- menubar-popover-5: NO functional change to MenuBarController.handleOpenWindow (:224-232). Per review this is no-op-safe (makeKeyAndOrderFront synchronously drives SwiftUI view/onReceive installation on the same main-actor turn before the enqueued Task runs, so the .openSession subscriber is normally registered first — downgraded to low/latent, not a demonstrated break). Do NOT add a retry, a second post, or pass an initial-session param into MainWindowView. Leave the cold-open ordering machinery absent; the source-scan test cannot assert cold-open timing, so there is nothing here to "prove a gap".
- onboarding-firstrun-3: Add an empty/indexing placeholder to PopoverView.timelineSection (:136-152): when recentSessions.isEmpty render an EmptyState-style row ("Indexing your sessions…" when serviceStatusStore.status == .starting, else "No sessions yet") instead of a blank scroll region.
- usage-cost-4-popover: Add the unconfigured-usage row INSIDE PopoverView.swift (which this WP owns), NOT in PopoverUsageSection.swift (owned by WP08; its body is fully gated on `if !usageData.isEmpty` at :19 with no else branch, so it renders nothing when empty). Render the muted "No usage data — set token limits in Settings" row as a sibling next to the existing `PopoverUsageSection(usageData:)` call at PopoverView.swift:23, gated on serviceStatusStore.usageData.isEmpty, posting .openSettings on tap (PopoverView already posts .openSettings at :42). Do NOT edit PopoverUsageSection.swift.

settings-ai-3 (Popover half): REMOVE embeddingStatusView (:66-76) and its statusDot from the popover header (the third dot at :59-60 bound to embeddingStatus), keeping only the Web and Service dots. The var embeddingStatus: String? field on EngramServiceStatusStore stays untouched.
- **Changes:**
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/Pages/HomeView.swift` — Wrap Sessions/Projects/Service KPICards in Buttons posting .navigateToScreen (.sessions/.projects/.settings); add trailingAction 'See all' to Continue/Follow-ups (->.sessions) and Changed Repos (->.projects) panels via a new optional WorkbenchPanel.trailingAction forwarded to SectionHeader, gated on count>limit (todayPanelRowLimit for Continue/Follow-ups, 5 for Changed Repos); add optional onTap to the private ServiceStateRow and make only the Web UI row open http://host:port/ via NSWorkspace when endpointPort != nil; REMOVE the 'brain' Embeddings ServiceStateRow and its serviceStatusStore.embeddingStatus binding + 'Check Advanced diagnostics' literal; add an 'Indexing…' EmptyState branch (icon arrow.triangle.2.circlepath) to the three workbench empty states keyed on serviceStatusStore.status==.starting; in ChangedRepoRow add a trailing tappable warning badge posting .navigateToScreen(.projects) when a warning exists, leaving row-open behavior intact.

- **APIs used:**
  - `.navigateToScreen / .openSession / .openWindow / .openSettings` (macos/Engram/AppNotifications.swift) `Notification.Name; navigateToScreen object is a Screen.rawValue String consumed in MainWindowView.onReceive; .openSession/.openWindow take a SessionBox object; .openSettings takes nil.   - `PopoverUsageSection` (macos/Engram/Views/Usage/PopoverUsageSection.swift) `struct PopoverUsageSection: View { let usageData: [EngramServiceUsageItem] }; body fully gated on `if !usageData.isEmpty` (:19) with NO else branch — renders nothing when empty, so the unconfigured row must live in PopoverView, NOT here (WP08-owned)` ✓
  - `openWebUI / web endpoint pattern` (macos/Engram/MenuBarController.swift) `openWebUI() (:287-293): host = serviceStatusStore.endpointHost ?? "127.0.0.1"; port = serviceStatusStore.endpointPort; URL(string: "http://\(host):\(port)/") then NSWorkspace.shared.open(url)` ✓

  - `PopoverView serviceClient injection` (macos/Engram/MenuBarController.swift) `PopoverView().environment(db).environment(serviceStatusStore).environment(serviceClient) at :47-53 — serviceClient already in the popover environment, so adding @Environment(EngramServiceClient.self) to PopoverView needs zero extra wiring` ✓
  - `handleOpenWindow` (macos/Engram/MenuBarController.swift) `@objc func handleOpenWindow(_:) (:224-232) — openWindow() then, if SessionBox, Task { @MainActor in post .openSession }. Left functionally UNCHANGED in this WP (menubar-popover-5 no-op-safe).` ✓
- **UX behavior:** Today KPI cards: Sessions/Projects/Service cards gain a pointer cursor and on click switch the main window to the Sessions / Projects / Settings screen respectively via .navigateToScreen. The "Today" card stays non-interactive. No visual restyle beyond the button hit area.
See-all links: each overflow panel header shows a trailing "See all ›" link ONLY when the loaded count exceeds the visible limit (Continue/Follow-ups > todayPanelRowLimit, Changed Repos > 5). Clicking navigates to Sessions (Continue/Follow-ups) or Projects (Changed Repos). When count ≤ limit, no link.
Web UI row: when endpointPort is non-nil, the row is tappable (pointer cursor, opens http://host:port/ in the default browser); when port is nil it shows "Unavailable" and is non-interactive.
Embeddings row/dot: removed entirely from both HomeView Service State and the popover header. No replacement text. The underlying store field is untouched.
Changed Repos warning: when a repo has a warning ('Migrated' / 'N changed · N unpushed'), the warning badge itself is tappable and navigates to the Projects page; tapping the rest of the row still opens the first transcript as today.
First-index vs empty: while serviceStatusStore.status == .starting, the three Today panels and the popover timeline show an "Indexing your sessions…" placeholder (icon arrow.triangle.2.circlepath) instead of the terminal "No …" copy. Once status is .running and counts are still 0, the terminal empty states show as before; panels fill progressively as the totalSessions-keyed reload re-runs.
Popover Live section: at the top, a "Live" header with the count of active sessions computed by the EXACT badge predicate (activityLevel == "active"), so the menu-bar ●N and the popover "N active" always match. Each live entry is a compact LiveSessionCard; an active session pulses green. Clicking a card whose sessionId is non-nil resolves the session off the main thread and opens the standalone window on it (post .openWindow(SessionBox)); cards with nil sessionId render plain and are not clickable. When there are no live sessions, the Live section is hidden (the badge also shows no ●N then, so they stay consistent).
Popover timeline discoverability: each historical row shows a trailing chevron, highlights its background on hover, and has an "Open session" tooltip; double-click still opens the window. Single-click intentionally does nothing.
Popover staleness: while the popover is open, a single 10s timer re-runs loadData (which also refetches the live section) so the recent list, "last Nm" label, and live count stay current; the timer is invalidated in .onDisappear.
Popover usage empty: when usageData is empty, a single muted row "No usage data — set token limits in Settings" appears in PopoverView; tapping it posts .openSettings. When usage data exists, the normal PopoverUsageSection renders unchanged (PopoverUsageSection itself is not modified).
Edge cases: nil endpointPort -> Web UI non-interactive; nil sessionId live card -> non-interactive; liveSessions() throws -> Live section hidden (silent, matches the badge's silent-fail); getSession returns nil / throws for a live session id -> no-op (no window opened, no crash); cold-open deep-link path is unchanged (warm path reliable, cold path low/latent per review).
- **Acceptance:**
  - Clicking the Sessions/Projects/Service KPI cards on Today navigates to the Sessions/Projects/Settings screen; the Today card does nothing.
  - Each Today overflow panel shows a 'See all ›' link only when its loaded count exceeds the visible row limit, and the link navigates to Sessions (Continue/Follow-ups) or Projects (Changed Repos).
  - The Today Web UI Service State row opens http://host:port/ in the browser when a port is available, and is non-interactive (shows 'Unavailable') when not.
  - The Embeddings Service State row is gone from HomeView and the Embedding status dot is gone from the popover header; no binding to serviceStatusStore.embeddingStatus remains in either view, while the store's embeddingStatus property itself is unchanged.
  - A Changed Repos row with a warning badge navigates to the Projects page when the badge is tapped; tapping elsewhere still opens the first transcript.
  - While serviceStatusStore.status == .starting, the three Today panels and the popover timeline show an 'Indexing…' placeholder distinct from the terminal 'No …' empty states.
  - The popover shows a Live section whose active-session count is computed with the same activityLevel == "active" predicate as MenuBarController.updateBadge (:409), so it equals the badge's ●N; the section is hidden when there are no live sessions.
  - A live-session card with a non-nil sessionId opens the standalone window on that session when clicked, resolving getSession off the main thread before posting .openWindow; a nil-sessionId card is non-interactive.
  - Popover historical timeline rows expose a chevron, hover highlight, and 'Open session' tooltip; double-click still opens the window.
  - While the popover stays open, a single 10s timer re-runs loadData (refreshing both the recent list and the live count) and is invalidated on disappear.
  - When usageData is empty, PopoverView shows a muted 'No usage data — set token limits in Settings' row that opens Settings on tap; PopoverUsageSection.swift is not modified.
- **Test plan:** Add macos/EngramTests/HomePopoverActionsTests.swift using the static source-scan pattern already established in ViewMainThreadReadTests.swift (repoRoot + source(_:) helpers read the .swift sources and assert on their text — the project convention for view-wiring tests that can't be unit-instantiated). Assertions: (1) HomeView.swift contains '.navigateToScreen' posts for the KPI buttons and the See-all trailingAction, and references Screen.sessions/.projects/.settings raw values; (2) HomeView.swift no longer contains 'embeddingStatus' or the 'Check Advanced diagnostics' literal and no longer has a 'brain' Embeddings ServiceStateRow; (3) HomeView.swift Changed Repos warning path posts .navigateToScreen(.projects); (4) HomeView.swift gates an 'Indexing' branch on '.starting'; (5) PopoverView.swift contains 'serviceClient.liveSessions()' and 'LiveSessionCard', filters 'activityLevel == \"active\"' for the live count, no longer contains 'embeddingStatus'/'embeddingStatusView', contains a '.help(' on the timeline row and an empty/indexing branch in timelineSection, and an .openSettings post gated on 'usageData.isEmpty'; (6) LiveSessionCard.swift exposes an 'onOpen' closure and guards interactivity on 'sessionId'. These mirror the existing ViewMainThreadReadTests source-assertion tests, so they run in the same EngramTests target with no new harness. (Per the established pattern, pure-logic helpers already have behavioral tests in TodayWorkbenchScopeTests; this WP adds no new pure helper, so source-scan wiring tests are the appropriate coverage. Note: the source scan cannot assert cold-open timing, consistent with menubar-popover-5 being a documented no-op.)
- **Risks:** Source-scan tests are brittle to renames/refactors but match the repo's existing test convention for view wiring; behavioral SwiftUI interaction tests aren't feasible here without a UI-test target. The single 10s popover timer must be invalidated in .onDisappear so it doesn't fire against a dismissed view. Adding a Live section that calls liveSessions() on every popover open + every 10s tick adds a recursive FS scan cost identical to what MenuBarController already does; acceptable since the popover is transient and the visible-only single timer keeps it bounded (MenuBarController also rate-limits its own scan, but the popover timer fires at most every 10s while visible). The live-count predicate is pinned to the exact badge predicate (activityLevel == \"active\") so menubar-popover-6 cannot drift; any future change to the badge predicate must update both call sites. The live-card open path resolves getSession off the main thread per the project read rule; a synchronous main-thread call would violate it. menubar-popover-5 is intentionally left as a no-op (review: low/latent, makeKeyAndOrderFront installs the subscriber before the enqueued post) — flagged so it isn't silently dropped, and no speculative ordering machinery is added. Removing the embedding UI bindings is safe because embeddingStatus has zero production writers (confirmed); the store property is left intact so EngramServiceStatusStoreTests is unaffected.
- **Out of scope:** Does NOT build any semantic/embedding capability — the product is keyword-only (CLAUDE.md: sqlite-vec not implemented); the Home/Popover embedding row+dot are removed (UI bindings only), not relabeled or backfilled, and the EngramServiceStatusStore.embeddingStatus property is deliberately left in place to avoid breaking EngramServiceStatusStoreTests. The serviceClient.embeddingStatus() IPC method (distinct from the store field, used by SearchPageView with its own @State) is not touched. The SearchPageView embedded-count pill (search-3) and the AISettingsSection embedding controls are owned by WP04 and are not touched here. Does NOT add pagination to the Sessions list (sessions-browse-2, different WP) — the See-all link just navigates to the existing page. Does NOT add session-level actions (Resume/Export/Handoff) to live cards or popover rows (xc-deadends / command-palette WPs); live cards get open-only. Does NOT change the badge computation in MenuBarController; it reuses the same activityLevel=='active' predicate so the popover stays consistent. Does NOT add a date-range/zoom or per-project filter to any surface. Does NOT modify PopoverUsageSection.swift (WP08-owned) — the empty-usage row lives in PopoverView. Does NOT modify MenuBarController.handleOpenWindow (menubar-popover-5 left as a documented no-op). No LiveSessionsView.swift file is created; the live UI reuses the existing LiveSessionCard inside PopoverView.

### WP10 — Dashboards drill-in: make Activity/Timeline/Repos/WorkGraph rows+charts open sessions; add file_activity to Activity; add loading/empty/error states

- **Disposition:** mixed  ·  **Critique:** needs-revision (revised)
- **Closes:** activity-1, activity-2, activity-3, activity-4, activity-5, timeline-1, timeline-2, timeline-3, timeline-4, workspace-repos-1, workspace-repos-2, workspace-repos-3, workspace-repos-4, workspace-repos-5, xc-deadends-7 (WorkGraphRow portion only), xc-states-1, xc-states-2
- **Goal:** Turn the four read-only dashboard pages (Activity, Timeline, Repos/RepoDetail, WorkGraph) into navigable entry points: By-Source rows, repo rows, related-session rows, and the WorkGraph repo rows drill into the underlying session(s)/repo via the existing .openSession notification or the existing RepoDetail nav; surface the existing file_activity backend on the Activity page as a display-only Top Files section; honor Timeline's chart/range/per-project promise; and give the pages consistent loading/empty/error states where they are still missing. Tighten RepoDetail's over-broad related-sessions match (it currently matches on project LIKE '%name%') and finish WorkGraph's honest relabel (icon/empty-copy/a11y still use graph framing even though the title was already changed to "Repo Activity").
- **Approach:** The drill-in primitive already exists and is used by every list page: `NotificationCenter.default.post(name: .openSession, object: SessionBox(session))`, handled in MainWindowView which sets selectedSession to open the transcript. TimelinePageView already uses it for card taps (lines 89/92), so the pattern is in-file proven. The whole WP is built on that one wire plus the standard SkeletonRow/EmptyState/AlertBanner state pattern siblings already use.

GROUND-TRUTH RECONCILIATION (from re-reading real code — the original spec over-claimed several already-done items):
- WorkGraphView.swift is ALREADY partially fixed: title is already "Repo Activity" (line 32), it already has `onRefresh`, an `AlertBanner` on error (lines 27-29), an `isLoading` flag, and an empty-state guarded by `repos.isEmpty && !isLoading` (lines 42-48). What REMAINS unfixed: (a) rows are NOT tappable (no Button, no selectedRepo / RepoDetail nav), (b) the SectionHeader icon is still `point.3.connected.trianglepath.dotted` (graph framing), (c) the EmptyState icon is still `point.3.connected.trianglepath.dotted` and copy still says "Work Graph builds as repos are discovered…", (d) accessibilityLabel is still "Work graph". So WP10's WorkGraph work shrinks to: add row drill-in + finish the icon/copy/a11y relabel. The KPI/AlertBanner/loading-empty-state work claimed in the original spec is already present — do NOT re-add it.
- ReposView.swift ALREADY has `isLoading`, `error`+AlertBanner, EmptyState guarded by `!isLoading`, and rows already drill into RepoDetail via RepoRow's Button → selectedRepo. The ONLY remaining gap (workspace-repos-4) is that no ProgressView renders while loading — the four KPI cards show zeros during the initial load. Same true gap exists in WorkGraphView. So workspace-repos-4 = add one ProgressView branch to each.
- getContext (Database.swift:611-624) primary clause is `project LIKE '%name%'` (substring on project NAME, not cwd); the `cwd LIKE '%cwd%'` is only the empty-result fallback (line 619). THIS is the over-match: a repo named "app" matches project "webhook-app", "my-app-v2", etc. `sessionsForRepo` with anchored `cwd LIKE path||'%'` fixes it.
- TimelinePageView already posts .openSession on card/child taps and already has `.task(id:)` cancellation, but has NO loadError state and NO AlertBanner — it only logs on failure (lines 130-132, 141, 157). It still hardcodes `sessionTimeline(days: 30)` (line 120) and a static "30d" badge (line 55).
- ActivityView already has loadError+AlertBanner (lines 13/18-20) and an `isLoading` flag, but renders NO loading affordance and NO empty state — it shows bare zeroed KPIs + empty charts on a fresh DB. By-Source rows render `SourcePill + Text` inside a plain HStack with `.padding(.vertical, 4)` (lines 34-43), NOT a Button.

CROSS-FILE BACKEND (additive read methods on macos/Engram/Core/Database.swift — see risks; needs orchestrator sign-off as a shared additive change):
- `getFileActivity` lives ONLY in EngramMCP/Core/MCPDatabase.swift (line 313) which the app target cannot call, so the app needs its own `fileActivity(...)` facade mirroring that exact SQL (SELECT sf.file_path, sf.action, SUM(sf.count) AS total_count, COUNT(DISTINCT sf.session_id) AS session_count FROM session_files sf JOIN sessions s ON s.id=sf.session_id [WHERE…] GROUP BY sf.file_path, sf.action ORDER BY total_count DESC LIMIT ?), guarded by `try Self.tableExists("session_files", db: db)` like listFavorites guards "favorites" (Database.swift:629). `tableExists` is `private static` on the same DatabaseManager type, so the new method can call it directly.
- workspace-repos-3 needs `sessionsForRepo(path:limit:)` using anchored cwd-prefix (`cwd LIKE ?` with arg `path + "%"`, NOT `%path%`) so RepoDetail stops reusing getContext's project-substring + unanchored-cwd-fallback match.
Both follow the existing `readInBackground` nonisolated convention; they add no app SQLite writers (reads only).

CORRECTION to expected APIs: there is NO `EngramServiceClient.listSessions` (only `liveSessions()`). All session reads go through `db.listSessions(sources:projects:since:includeHidden:subAgent:topLevelOnly:sort:limit:offset:)` on DatabaseManager (confirmed, line 171). MCPDatabase.getFileActivity is reference SQL only — the app uses the new `db.fileActivity` facade.

- **UX behavior:** DRILL-IN:
- Activity By-Source row tap: opens the single most-recent session for that source (db.listSessions(sources:[source], sort:.updatedDesc, limit:1).first). 0 visible sessions (race) → silent no-op (no crash, no alert). The Button uses .buttonStyle(.plain) so the existing SourcePill + count + .padding(.vertical, 4) styling is preserved with no button chrome.
- Activity daily chart: now a source-stacked StackedActivityChart (segmented by source). It is display-only — NO per-bar / per-day drill-in (cut as speculative; activity-1 only requires By-Source rows to be tappable).
- Top Files rows: display-only (file_path basename + action 'edit'/'read' + total count). The file_activity payload carries no session id, so rows do NOT navigate and render with no chevron / no Button styling — an informational section, not a dead clickable-looking control.
- RepoDetail related-session row tap: opens that session's transcript (.openSession). Pointer cursor; matches the card styling that already implied tappability.
- WorkGraphRow tap: drills into RepoDetailView for that repo (selectedRepo), which itself drills to sessions. Back button returns to the WorkGraph list. (This is the WorkGraphRow portion of xc-deadends-7 ONLY; LiveSessionCard and SourcePulseView per-source rows are owned by WP09/WP13 and are NOT touched here.)

STATES:
- Activity loading: while isLoading && dailyActivity.isEmpty → ProgressView instead of zeroed KPIs + empty charts. Empty (fresh DB): EmptyState('No activity yet — Indexed sessions will appear here'). Error: existing AlertBanner (kept).
- Timeline loading: ProgressView while isLoading && timeline.isEmpty. Empty: existing EmptyState, but gated to render only when timeline.isEmpty && loadError == nil && !isLoading. Error: new AlertBanner ('Failed to load timeline: …') shown instead of the misleading 'No sessions in the last 30 days'; confirm/dismiss IPC failures also surface via this banner instead of silently logging.
- Repos / WorkGraph loading: ProgressView while isLoading && repos.isEmpty, instead of four 0-value KPI cards. (error AlertBanner + EmptyState already present in both.)
- RepoDetail: isLoading gate prevents a false-empty flash; after load, a muted 'No recent sessions for this repo' line shows when relatedSessions is empty (and optionally a one-line 'No CLAUDE.md found').

TIMELINE CONTROLS:
- Range picker (7/30/90/All): changing it cancels the in-flight load (.task(id:)) and reloads with the new days; the badge text updates to match (no more static '30d'). 'All' uses a large days value (~100000).
- Project picker: 'All Projects' default; selecting a project filters the already-loaded timeline client-side (no extra query). Selected project with no sessions in range → empty state.
- Chart band: a small ActivityChart of per-day counts sits above the grouped list, visualizing volume so the 'Timeline' name/chart icon is no longer a broken promise.

EDGE CASES: missing/empty cwd → sessionsForRepo prefix match returns []; RepoDetail shows the empty placeholder. service-busy/db-locked during reindex → load throws → AlertBanner; no blank-stale page. session_files table absent (older DB) → fileActivity returns [] (tableExists guard) → Top Files section omitted, not an error.
- **Acceptance:**
  - Tapping a By-Source row on the Activity page opens a session transcript (the most-recent session for that source); a source with no sessions is a no-op, not a crash; SourcePill styling and .padding(.vertical,4) are preserved (Button is .plain).
  - The Activity page shows a Top Files section listing file_path basename / action / counts from db.fileActivity when session_files has data, and omits the section (no error) when the table is absent or empty. Rows are display-only (no chevron, no navigation).
  - The Activity page shows a ProgressView while loading and an EmptyState (not bare zeros + blank charts) on a fresh/empty DB; the existing error AlertBanner still fires on load failure.
  - Activity's daily chart renders StackedActivityChart fed by db.dailySourceActivity (orphan view + previously test-only query now wired); grep for StackedActivityChart shows a real view caller. ActivityChart.swift is NOT modified.
  - RepoDetail 'Recent Sessions' rows are tappable and open the session transcript via .openSession.
  - RepoDetail related sessions come from sessionsForRepo (anchored cwd-prefix); a repo whose path is '/Users/a/app' no longer surfaces sessions whose cwd is '/Users/a/webhook' OR '/Users/a/app-v2'.
  - RepoDetail shows a muted 'No recent sessions' placeholder when empty, only after load resolves (no false-empty flash).
  - WorkGraphRow rows are tappable and drill into RepoDetailView; WorkGraph's in-page SectionHeader icon, EmptyState icon+copy, and accessibilityLabel no longer use graph framing (title was already 'Repo Activity').
  - ReposView and WorkGraphView show a ProgressView while loading (isLoading && repos.isEmpty) instead of four zeroed KPI cards.
  - Timeline has a working range picker (7/30/90/All) that re-queries sessionTimeline(days:) and updates the badge; a project picker that filters the list client-side; a chart band above the list; a ProgressView while loading; and a new AlertBanner on load failure that prevents the misleading empty state, also surfacing confirm/dismiss failures.
  - All new behavior compiles, xcodebuild Debug succeeds, and the new XCTest file passes. xc-deadends-7 is closed ONLY for the WorkGraphRow surface (LiveSessionCard/SourcePulseView remain WP09/WP13).
- **Test plan:** Add macos/EngramTests/DashboardDrillInTests.swift (XCTest, @testable import Engram), reusing the createSessionsTable + DatabaseManagerTests-style temp-DB setUp (dbPath + DatabaseManager.open). The session_files table is created inline in the test (the create-extension-table-in-test pattern, like insertFavorite for favorites):
1. testFileActivityReturnsAggregatedRows: CREATE TABLE session_files(session_id TEXT, file_path TEXT, action TEXT, count INTEGER); insert one session (via insertTestSession) + two file rows (edit/read) → assert db.fileActivity(project:nil, since:nil, limit:10) returns rows with correct totalCount (SUM) / sessionCount (COUNT DISTINCT), ordered by total_count DESC.
2. testFileActivityReturnsEmptyWhenTableAbsent: temp DB WITHOUT session_files → db.fileActivity(...) returns [] and does NOT throw (tableExists guard).
3. testFileActivityProjectAndSinceFilters: insert two sessions in different projects/times + their file rows → assert project and since filters scope the result.
4. testSessionsForRepoUsesAnchoredCwdPrefix: because insertTestSession HARDCODES cwd '/Users/test/project' (TestHelpers line 133, no cwd param), insert these rows with RAW-SQL INSERT supplying all NOT NULL columns (id, source, start_time, file_path; project nullable) and varying cwd: '/Users/a/app', '/Users/a/webhook', AND '/Users/a/app-v2' (the trailing-collision row that actually proves anchoring beats getContext's substring/unanchored bug) → assert db.sessionsForRepo(path:'/Users/a/app') returns ONLY the '/Users/a/app' session, NOT 'webhook' and NOT 'app-v2'.
5. testSessionsForRepoExcludesHidden: a hidden session (hidden_at NOT NULL) under the repo cwd is not returned.
(SwiftUI state/drill-in rendering is exercised only at the read layer here; the .openSession wiring reuses the verified MainWindowView handler and the in-file TimelinePageView precedent, so coverage focuses on the two new data contracts the views depend on.)
- **Risks:** FILE CONFLICT (HARD, must resolve before starting Timeline edits): macos/Engram/Views/Pages/TimelinePageView.swift is listed in BOTH WP01's and WP10's owned-file sets, and WP10 actively edits it (timeline-1/2/3/4 + xc-states-2 all modify it). Two WPs cannot concurrently own/edit one file. The verbatim finding evidence (timeline-1/2/3/4, xc-states-2) all point at TimelinePageView, so WP10 is the natural owner; WP01's listing appears stale and should be removed from WP01. Until the orchestrator confirms WP10 ownership, the TimelinePageView edits are GATED (the other four files are independent and can proceed).

CROSS-FILE BACKEND APPROVAL GATE: activity-2 (fileActivity) and workspace-repos-3 (sessionsForRepo) add two ADDITIVE read methods to macos/Engram/Core/Database.swift, which is OUT of WP10's owned-file set. Per the WP map, Database.swift (the APP DatabaseManager) is not in any other WP's owned set, so additive read-only methods there are safe and collision-free — but because the file is shared/unowned, this addition needs explicit orchestrator sign-off as a shared additive change rather than an assumption. No app SQLite writers are added (reads only), so the ServiceWriterGate rule is respected.

xc-deadends-7 SCOPE (do not over-claim): the finding spans three surfaces — WorkGraphRow (WP10-owned), LiveSessionCard (macos/Engram/Components/LiveSessionCard.swift, WP09-owned), and SourcePulseView per-source rows (macos/Engram/Views/Pages/SourcePulseView.swift, WP13-owned). WP10 closes ONLY the WorkGraphRow portion; the finding is NOT fully closed by WP10. findingsCovered lists it as 'xc-deadends-7 (WorkGraphRow portion only)'.

activity-5 DECISION RISK: the spec wires StackedActivityChart (the finding's 'ship the richer view' option) rather than deleting it; the visible daily chart changes from single-color to source-stacked. If review prefers strict removal, fall back to deleting StackedActivityChart + leaving dailySourceActivity unused. Wiring is the lower-risk default (no dead-code deletion, gives source segmentation for free).

workspace-repos-2 SCOPE: only the in-page icon/empty-state/accessibility copy is relabeled (the title was already 'Repo Activity'). The screen/tab title 'Work Graph' and its nav icon live in macos/Engram/Models/Screen.swift (NOT owned) — out of scope. Rendering a real node/edge graph is explicitly deferred.

timeline-4 SCOPE: per-project filtering is client-side over the loaded 7/30/90/All-day window (sessionTimeline has no project param). For very large 'All' ranges this loads more sessions into memory than a server-side filter would; acceptable given the read is off-main and bounded by the existing tier/hidden filters. A server-side project param is the durable fix (deferred to avoid a non-owned Database.swift signature change).

Drill-in precision: Activity source taps open the single most-recent session rather than a pre-filtered Sessions list, because SessionsPageView holds its filters in local @State with no deep-link channel and is NOT owned. Opening the representative session is the minimum honest drill-in.
- **Out of scope:** Does NOT: (1) build semantic/vector file search or any backend beyond the two additive read facades; (2) add a deep-linked pre-filtered Sessions list from Activity/charts (no SessionsPageView deep-link channel exists and SessionsPageView is not owned) — taps open the representative most-recent session; (3) add per-bar / per-day chart drill-in on Activity or Timeline (CUT as speculative — no finding requires it; activity-1 only needs By-Source rows tappable); (4) edit ActivityChart.swift — the speculative optional onTapDay closure on StackedActivityChart/ActivityChart is CUT; both views are reused unchanged; (5) render a real node/edge relationship graph for WorkGraph (relabel only); (6) rename the 'Work Graph' nav tab/icon in Screen.swift (not owned); (7) add a server-side project parameter to sessionTimeline (timeline-4 done client-side); (8) make Top Files rows navigate (the file_activity payload has no session id); (9) re-add WorkGraph/Repos title, AlertBanner, or empty-state that ALREADY exist in the real code; (10) close the LiveSessionCard or SourcePulseView portions of xc-deadends-7 (WP09/WP13); (11) wire the four dead context-menu actions (Resume/Handoff/Replay/Copy) on Timeline cards (xc-deadends-1/replay-4, a different WP).

### WP11 — Projects: migration-history view + batch-move + alias add/remove UI; replace non-shipping `engram` CLI guidance with honest in-app copy

- **Disposition:** mixed  ·  **Critique:** needs-revision (revised)
- **Closes:** projects-migration-1, projects-migration-2, projects-migration-3, projects-migration-4, projects-migration-5, xc-capability-matrix-10
- **Goal:** Surface the project-migration backend the app already reaches (browsable migration history, batch move, alias add/remove) inside the Projects view, and remove every `engram project ...` CLI command reference from the Projects sheets. Defer the parts whose backend is MCP-only (recover/review/timeline) rather than fabricate a wire-up that cannot compile.
- **Approach:** Grounded reality (re-verified by reading source after the adversarial critique): the Projects views inject the CONCRETE EngramServiceClient via @Environment(EngramServiceClient.self), so any concrete method on that class is callable from a view. Three of the WP's "expected APIs" are reachable, three are NOT.

REACHABLE (wire-up):
- projectMigrations(EngramServiceProjectMigrationsRequest(state:limit:)) -> EngramServiceProjectMigrationsResponse. Method on EngramServiceClient; DTOs live in macos/Shared/Service/EngramServiceModels.swift (Request:882, Response:887, EngramServiceMigrationLogEntry:891 with id/oldPath/newPath/oldBasename/newBasename/state/startedAt/finishedAt?/archived/auditNote?/actor/detail?). Today only consumed as an Undo picker (state:"committed",limit:5) and an enablement probe (limit:1).
- projectMoveBatch(EngramServiceProjectMoveBatchRequest(yaml:dryRun:force:actor:)) -> EngramServiceJSONValue. Method on EngramServiceClient (concrete-only; NOT in EngramServiceClientProtocol/Mock — fine, the view uses the concrete client and I test via a local stub transport). Request DTO at EngramServiceModels.swift:700 (yaml; dry_run; force; actor?).
  CRITICAL DRY-RUN CONTRACT (corrected per critique, verified at EngramServiceCommandHandler+ProjectMigration.swift:127-160 + EngramCoreWrite/ProjectMove/Batch.swift:195-205,268): the batch handler IGNORES request.dryRun. It builds BatchOverrides(force: request.force) only (Batch.swift BatchOverrides:100-114 has NO dryRun field), and Batch.run passes dryRun: doc.defaults.dryRun (Batch.swift:268), which is parsed exclusively from the JSON body's defaults.dry_run / defaults.dryRun (Batch.swift:195-199, default false). So dry-run for BATCH is driven ONLY by the JSON body, never by the request-level field. BatchMoveSheet MUST encode {"version":1,"defaults":{"dry_run":true},"operations":[...]} for Preview and omit/false defaults.dry_run for Commit. Relying on EngramServiceProjectMoveBatchRequest.dryRun would silently COMMIT real moves during 'Preview'. (Contrast projectMove/projectArchive at lines 26/61/69/80 DO honor request.dryRun — that asymmetry is what misled the original design.)
  Per-operation schema (verified Batch.swift:146-187): each op needs src (non-empty) plus exactly one of dst (non-empty) | archive:true (XOR enforced at :169). For batch move we always emit {src,dst}. Response (verified encodeBatchResult at EngramServiceCommandHandler+ProjectMigration.swift:257-290) is snake_case: {completed:[{migration_id,state,src,dst,files_patched,occurrences,sessions_updated}], failed:[{src,dst,archive,error}], skipped:[{src,dst,archive}]}.
  EngramServiceJSONValue (EngramServiceModels.swift:3-45) is a BARE enum with NO accessors/subscript. Parsing the response into counts must hand-pattern-match: case .object(let dict), then for each key case .array(let items) -> items.count, and for failed entries case .object pull "src"/"error" via case .string. This is a small private helper in BatchMoveSheet, written by hand — not property access.
- manageProjectAlias(EngramServiceProjectAliasRequest(action:oldProject:newProject:actor:)) -> EngramServiceJSONValue. Method in protocol+mock; Request DTO at EngramServiceModels.swift:686 (action; old_project; new_project; actor?). Service handler (EngramServiceCommandHandler.swift:991-1027) supports action=="add"|"remove" only; there is NO "list" path on the service (list is MCP-only). CRITICAL (corrected per critique, verified at EngramServiceCommandHandler.swift:1002-1005): a SINGLE guard requires BOTH old_project AND new_project to be non-nil for BOTH add AND remove. So the AliasSheet REMOVE call must pass newProject:<projectName> (NOT nil) or the service throws invalidRequest("old_project and new_project are required"). Add: oldProject:<aliasInput>, newProject:<projectName>. Remove: oldProject:<aliasInput>, newProject:<projectName>. Response: .object([ok,action,alias,canonical,actor]).

NOT REACHABLE (defer / remove-misleading):
- projectRecover / projectReview / service-side projectTimeline DO NOT EXIST on EngramServiceClient — they live only in EngramMCP (MCPDatabase/MCPFileTools). The app's Database.projectTimeline is an unrelated local activity query returning [TimelineEntry], not migration recovery. Wiring these would require new service commands + handlers + protocol + mock entries across files this WP doesn't own. So projects-migration-5's recover/review-action and "show remaining files" disclosure are DEFERRED, not built.

Therefore the design:
1) projects-migration-1: new MigrationHistoryView sheet calling projectMigrations(state:nil,limit:100), rendering oldBasename->newBasename, full paths, humanized startedAt, actor, state badge, archived badge, auditNote. Reuse shared AlertBanner + EmptyState (verified to exist at macos/Engram/Components/AlertBanner.swift and EmptyState.swift) for error/empty states instead of hand-rolling banners. Copy UndoSheet's three timestamp formatters + humanizeMigrationTimestamp helper locally (UndoSheet.swift:13-37) — copied, not refactored, per the rules. Opened from a new "History…" toolbar button.
2) projects-migration-2 + xc-capability-matrix-10 (batch, severity LOW — KEEP MINIMAL): add a selection-mode toggle; when >=1 project selected show "Move Selected (n)…" opening a minimal BatchMoveSheet. ONE editable destination path per selected project (reverse-resolved via projectCwds). Build the JSON body the backend parses, call projectMoveBatch. Preview = body with defaults.dry_run:true; Commit = body without it (or false). On commit success post .projectsDidChange and dismiss. TRIMMED per critique: no per-operation re-preview loop and no elaborate partial-failure recovery UX — Preview shows completed/failed/skipped counts (and failed src+error lines), Commit either succeeds (dismiss) or surfaces an error banner; projects with no recorded cwd render as disabled 'no recorded path — skipped' rows. That is the minimum for a LOW finding.
3) projects-migration-3 + xc-capability-matrix-10 (alias): add an "Aliases…" item to the per-row Menu and .contextMenu opening AliasSheet for that project. Add field (action:"add", oldProject:<aliasInput>, newProject:<projectName>) and Remove field (action:"remove", oldProject:<aliasInput>, newProject:<projectName>). It does NOT list existing aliases (service has no list path) — an honest inline note states aliases can be added/removed but not enumerated in-app.
4) projects-migration-4 (remove-misleading): replace the four `engram project ...` CLI command strings — RenameSheet.swift:81 (`engram project move`) & :397 (`engram project review`), ArchiveSheet.swift:177 (`engram project review`), UndoSheet.swift:314 (`engram project review`) — with honest in-app copy (re-run the move, or open Migration History). NOTE: ArchiveSheet:56 and RenameSheet:81 also contain the phrase "engram can't locate it on disk" where "engram" is the APP NAME, not a CLI command; the grep guard targets the substring "engram project" so it does not flag the app-name usage. (RenameSheet:81 contains BOTH the app-name phrase and the `engram project move` CLI phrase in one string — only the CLI clause is removed.)
5) projects-migration-5 (defer): document that recover/review/timeline remain MCP-only; the residual-refs copy fix from (4) is the in-app honesty fix. No backend added.

All edits confined to ProjectsView.swift + the three CLI-string sheets + three new view files under macos/Engram/Views/Projects/ (auto-included by xcodegen) + one new test file. No other WP touches Projects.
- **Changes:**
  - `edit` `macos/Engram/Views/Pages/ProjectsView.swift` — Add a 'History…' toolbar button (opens MigrationHistoryView via new @State showHistorySheet). Add multi-select: @State selectedProjects: Set<String>, a 'Select'/'Done' toggle, leading row checkboxes in selection mode, and a 'Move Selected (n)…' button that opens BatchMoveSheet(projects:) when selectedProjects is non-empty.
